▲ Disaster Situation in the Lower Canal Region The eight counties of the Lower Canal region, including Jiangdu, Gaoyou, Baoying, Xinghua, Taixian, Dongtai, Yancheng, and Fumin, are bounded by the abandoned Yellow River to the north, the Tongyang Canal to the south, the sea to the east, and the eastern embankment of the Lower Canal to the west, which protects against the floodwaters of the Huai River. Whenever the dams leading to the Yangtze River are insufficient to discharge the water, the dams leading to the sea are opened, using the Lower Canal region to discharge into the sea. The Lower Canal is one or two zhang below the water level of the Lower Canal, and there are no major rivers to drain the water. Furthermore, the Fan Gong embankment obstructs the flow. The coastal areas are higher than the hinterland of the Lower Canal, preventing smooth flow into the sea. Therefore, even in years when only the dams leading to the sea are opened, the Lower Canal region must retain the Huai River floodwater for four or five days. This year's rainfall has been particularly heavy, and the low-lying areas of the Lower Canal region were already full. In addition, the Xin San Dam south of Cheluo was opened on August 24th, releasing a massive flow of 2,300 cubic meters per second, which accumulated for twenty-three days, and the people's lives were already unbearable. On the morning of August 26th, the canal embankment breached in twenty-seven locations, totaling 8,000 feet, and the water from Gaobao Lake flowed eastward in full force. By September 2nd, the water level of the Canal had dropped sharply by eight feet, turning the plains along the Lower Canal into a vast swamp. The loss of life and property is incalculable (awaiting further investigation).

▲ Relief Methods The severity and impact of this disaster caused by the breach of the eastern embankment of the Lower Canal are as described above. Therefore, relief measures must be planned and implemented promptly to save the millions of victims in the eight counties of the Lower Canal region. The resettlement of refugees, food supply, preparation of cotton-padded clothing, and all relief efforts for winter and spring are already being planned and implemented by the National Flood Relief Committee and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, so there is no need to elaborate further. The immediate measures that should be taken to repair the breaches in the eastern embankment of the Lower Canal, implement drainage projects in the Lower Canal region, renovate the western and eastern embankments of the Lower Canal, and expedite the diversion of Huai River water into the Yangtze River and the sea, are described separately below:

(A) Repairing the Breaches in the Eastern Embankment The eastern embankment of the Lower Canal has a total of twenty-seven breaches, large and small, with a total length of about 8,000 feet. Except for two breaches near the Six Gates that have dried up, and seven breaches in the southern section of Shaobo, as well as the breaches south and north of Wanshou Palace, which have also dried up, there are still over 6,000 feet of breaches with a strong eastward flow. Among them, the breaches north of Zhaoguan Dam, Lotus Pond in Lower Head, Lai Sheng Convent, Thirty Shops, Little Cheluo South, Seven Dukes Hall, Temple Alley Entrance, and Resist the Army Tower are the longest and most dangerous. The breaches have been scoured for a long time, and there is a fear that they will be level with the canal bed. In the future, not only will there be overspill at medium water levels, but it will also be difficult to stop the flow even at low water levels. If measures are not taken to close the breaches as soon as possible, this year's autumn harvest will be hopeless, and next year's planting will also be impossible. Houses cannot be repaired, and the people of the eight counties will have nowhere to live. The livelihood crisis may lead to nationwide unrest. However, the cost of repairing the breaches, using the old method of wood and earth for the smaller breaches and modern methods for the larger breaches, using wooden frames and rubble to close them, may require more than two million yuan (detailed figures to be estimated). It is feared that the Jiangsu Provincial Government will not be able to raise the funds in a short period. It is now known that the Central Government has established a National Flood Relief Committee to raise relief funds, and there is a proposal to issue a large amount of public bonds. To relieve the flood disaster in the Lower Canal region, repairing the breaches in the eastern embankment of the Lower Canal is of utmost importance. It is proposed that the National Government order the National Flood Relief Committee to take immediate responsibility for this breach repair project. We should also learn from the time-consuming experience of purchasing and transporting stones for repairing the Yongding River breach in Hebei Province eighteen years ago and start bidding for large pieces of rubble in advance. Once the water level drops slightly and work can begin, the breaches should be closed simultaneously, with the goal of closing all breaches in the shortest possible time. (B) Drainage Project for the Lower Canal Region Currently, the water depth in the Lower Canal region averages about six or seven feet, and the breaches continue to flow eastward. Before the breaches are closed, the water level will continue to rise. Since the ports to the sea are extremely congested, if drainage projects are not implemented during the retention period, it is feared that the land will not dry out before the heavy rains of next summer and autumn, let alone allow for planting this autumn and spring. Therefore, for the sake of the people's survival and the national economy, it is necessary to implement the drainage project for the Lower Canal region as soon as possible. As mentioned in the previous section, the Jiangsu Provincial Government may not be able to afford it for the time being. This drainage project is also an urgent task for relieving the flood disaster in the Lower Canal region. Therefore, it is also proposed that the National Government order the National Flood Relief Committee to handle it properly and quickly. The scope of the project includes dredging the ports to the sea to facilitate flow into the sea (and building sluice gates at the estuaries to prevent saltwater intrusion for long-term benefit), and opening more diversion canals into the ports, so that the land of the eight counties in the Lower Canal region can be dried out in the shortest possible time. (C) Renovation of the Eastern Embankment and Repair of the Western Embankment of the Lower Canal The eastern embankment of the Lower Canal has breached in twenty-seven locations because the embankments have been in disrepair for years, are incomplete, and have too many gaps. The main current directly impacts the eastern embankment of the Lower Canal, causing severe scouring at every curve. At the highest flood levels, the lakes and canals are connected. When strong northwesterly winds and waves occur, they cross the eastern embankment and scour its back. The insufficient height of the eastern embankment is obvious. Since the diversion of the Huai River into the Yangtze River and the sea has not been completed, the eastern embankment of the Lower Canal will continue to bear the responsibility of protecting the eight counties of the Lower Canal region. Therefore, it must be raised and thickened to prevent any eventuality. Straightening the dangerous curves will also benefit navigation and prevent scouring. The incomplete sections of the western embankment must be repaired to prevent waves from obstructing the canal during high water periods and endangering the eastern embankment. Even sections without breaches should be raised to prevent lake water from crossing the embankment. The outer slope of the western embankment, which faces the lake, already has stone protection. Stones should be added to areas without stones or with too few stones to prevent scouring. (D) The Huai River Regulation Project Should Commence Soon The problems of the Lower Canal and the disasters in the Lower Canal region this year and in the past stem from the fact that the channels for the Huai River to enter the Yangtze River have not been improved, and the channels to enter the sea have not been opened. As mentioned before, for fundamental relief, regulating the Huai River is the precursor to managing the Canal. The plans for diverting the Huai River into the Yangtze River and the sea are ready. If they can be implemented and completed soon, the problems of the Lower Canal will be solved easily, without the need for further discussion.

Record of the Current Survey of the Liyang Eastern Dam 65

The Liyang Eastern Dam is the lifeline of the Taihu Lake basin. Once it breaches, the Jian and Yu rivers will flow straight down, and the southern counties will be in danger of being submerged. Recently, due to continuous rains causing disasters and the collapse of the canal embankment, the Gao and Shao areas are lamenting. The people of the southern counties are very concerned about the safety of the Eastern Dam. It is widely rumored in the Xichang area that the Eastern Dam is in danger of breaching, causing rumors to spread and people to panic. The Liyang County Government, together with the Construction Bureau and local figures, took measuring instruments to the Eastern Dam on the 7th to conduct the latest survey. The survey situation is recorded as follows, which is also what those who care about the safety of the Eastern Dam want to see.

▲ Location and Current Situation of the Eastern Dam The Eastern Dam is located about seventy li west of Liyang County, in Gaochun County. It used to be a place where the Yangtze River flowed through. Later, because the Taihu Lake basin suffered repeated disasters, a dam was built to cut off the river flow. It is divided into upper and lower dams, ten li apart. The Eastern Dam is its general name. Director Shi and others departed at 6:00 AM on the 7th, traveling west along the Wen River from Nandun. The embankments on both sides were submerged, leaving no trace. The victims stood naked, in great pain. Passing through the Three Pagodas and Shengping ponds, these places used to be wide and relaxed stretches of the river. After the dam was built, the flow was cut off, and the ponds also silted up. Residents competed to plant rice and wheat, gradually turning them into farmland. Only a shallow river channel remained, barely connected. Now, it is a vast expanse of water, with surging waves. We silently thought to ourselves, if we could deepen these ponds to store water, it would be a benefit for the Taihu Lake basin for generations to come. Arriving at the Lower Dam in Dingbu, Anhui, it was already 2:00 PM. The residents along the dam were bustling and showed no signs of panic. After inspecting the dam body, it was as solid as usual. We immediately walked along the middle river to the Upper Dam. The middle river is ten li long, and the fields on both sides are quite high. Early rice has matured. Looking around, the scenery is beautiful. The residents on both sides were celebrating a bumper harvest. We arrived at the Upper Dam at 3:30 PM. Prosperity was even greater than the Lower Dam. At this time, the water west of the dam was level with the top of the dam. It had once overflowed the dam, but it was not a major problem. We then inspected the dam body, which was very intact. However, a few residents had built houses on top of the dam. The wall bases and wooden piles caused the stones to crack, which was very dangerous. We immediately used a leveling instrument to measure the difference in water level between the upper and lower dams and returned.

▲ Measurement Results The upper dam water level differed by 2.7 meters, and the lower dam water level differed by 6.8 meters, for a total difference of 9.58 feet, or about three zhang. This shows the huge difference in water potential. If it were to breach, the disaster in the southern counties would be even greater than in Jiangbei. The water from the middle river had already flowed into the Liu Gong Bridge in the Lower Dam. A small earthen dam has been built to block it.

▲ Current Situation Observation According to the current situation, the Eastern Dam is absolutely safe. However, there are a few points that should be noted: (A) Building houses on top of the dam should be prohibited. Those that have already been built should be demolished to avoid artificial damage. (B) The downstream counties, such as Sucheng, Xiyi, Liyang, etc., should jointly send a commissioner to be stationed there. Since the Eastern Dam was built in Gaochun, more than 100,000 mu of farmland has been submerged. There has always been a desire to gather people to excavate. Recently, rumors have spread again, saying that special actions are scheduled. Although they are unfounded, it is also important to plan ahead to prevent any eventuality. (C) Downstream counties should jointly raise annual repair funds (The Eastern Dam originally had annual repair funds, but they have been diverted due to military affairs). As the matter concerns the interests of the entire Taihu Lake basin, they should jointly raise funds, set the custody method, and use them for annual repairs to make a major plan for the future.

Please handle the matter. Yesterday, we sent personnel to Xiyi to report the survey situation and discuss future measures.

Tragic Situation of the Flood Disaster in Northern Jiangxi 66

Nanchang-Xunyang Railway Suspended for Half a Month

Relief Society Plans Relief Efforts

Nanchang News: Since early July, Jiujiang, Xingzi, Hukou, Pengze, Ruichang, Yongxiu, Xiushui, De'an, etc. in northern Jiangxi, as well as Poyang, Duchang, and Yugan counties near Poyang Lake, have been flooded one after another. By early August, the floodwaters had increased dramatically. Jiujiang City was several feet deep in water. The Yangtze River water level reached over forty-five feet. The Nanchang-Xunyang Railway was suspended for half a month because the floodwaters had damaged the roadbed. The water had also submerged the Saihu Yangliuqing area, resulting in losses of over 100,000 yuan. Although the floodwaters in Jiujiang have receded slightly, the retreat is very slow. The Nanchang-Xunyang Railway is now barely operating once a day (the morning express train has been suspended for over a month), but the small number of trains, the large number of passengers, and the slow travel speed have caused the passengers great suffering. According to those who came from Xunbu, the flood disaster in Jiujiang is extremely tragic. The embankments along the river have completely collapsed. Grain and livestock have been washed away. The number of collapsed houses and drowned people is countless. According to the report from the De'an Disaster Relief Committee: (A) In the first district, 3,880 households in twenty-five villages were flooded, and fifty people were drowned. The embankments of ten places, including Datang Lake, Gucun Lake, and Huying Jia Lake, were completely collapsed. The flooded paddy fields in the whole district were about 25,600 mu. 320 houses were collapsed by water in the whole district. 523 cattle and 943 pigs were drowned. (B) In the second district, 1,139 households in twelve villages were flooded, and more than forty people were drowned. More than 3,800 mu of fields and 800 mu of land were flooded. 180 houses were collapsed by water in the whole district. Seven hundred pigs and cattle were drowned. (C) In the third district, 735 households in twenty-five villages were flooded, and three people were drowned. 1,570 mu of fields were flooded. Six houses were collapsed. One hundred and thirty cattle and pigs were drowned. (D) In the fourth district, 666 households in twenty-four villages were flooded. 1,320 mu of fields were flooded. Ten houses were destroyed. More than thirty pigs and cattle were drowned. According to the Relief Committee, after the bandit disaster in the province, a flood disaster occurred again. The disaster victims are scattered across northern Jiangxi. After the flood recedes, how to resettle the millions of victims is a major problem. Other provinces have only flood disasters, but this province has bandit disasters throughout the eighty-one counties. Looking around the province, there is almost no clean land. Currently, the Relief Committee is planning the following measures: (1) Request the National Government to issue flood disaster public bonds, because after the bandit disaster in the province, the treasury is empty and there are no funds to allocate. Sporadic fundraising is useless. (2) Provide relief through work projects. Nearby refugees will repair the collapsed embankments in various places. If this cannot fully accommodate all the refugees, then build provincial and county roads. At the same time, try to supplement planting of short-term miscellaneous grains and vegetables. (3) The Water Conservancy Bureau of the Construction Department will send more technicians to various disaster areas to carry out various industrial relief efforts to promote production while providing disaster relief.

The Provincial Government believes that the flood disaster in this province is serious. In addition to requesting relief from the Central Government and other parties, Chairman Lu is traveling to Beijing with a flood disaster report to report the disaster situation in the province to the Central Government. The Provincial Relief Committee has allocated the remaining 90,000 yuan of relief funds to various counties for emergency relief. Public groups in the province, considering the large number of victims and the severity of the disaster, are raising funds for disaster relief. The Jiangxi Provincial Flood Disaster Relief Association, initiated by the Provincial Federation of Industry and Commerce, held its first preparatory meeting yesterday, and decided that the Provincial Federation of Industry and Commerce's communications office, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Jiangxi Charity Federation would send telegrams to the Central Party Department, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Interior, the Flood Relief Committee, and the Relief Committee, requesting immediate relief. Hu Youyu, Zeng Jinshan, Lu Fuchuang, Xu Ruifu and other five people were publicly elected to visit He Yingqin at the headquarters to ask for instructions on all relief measures for the flood disaster.

(9th)

Hubei Relief Organizations Define Authority 67

Hankou News: Wuhan has been flooded for more than a month. Although the floodwaters have gradually receded in recent days, they have receded by less than a foot. The water level is still over fifty-one feet. In the cool autumn September, the weather has changed suddenly, and millions of victims are suffering greatly. The victims in the other counties are even worse. Now, after the Civil Affairs Department has conducted another investigation and distinguished the severity of the disaster, it has designated the following disaster areas: The first-class disaster areas are Wuchang, Hanyang, Yunmeng, Xiaogan, Huangkang, Mianyang, Hanchuan, Guangji, Huangmei, Shishou, Tianmen, Jiangling, Echeng, and Jianli, for a total of fourteen counties. The second-class disaster areas are Yingcheng, Qishui, Huanggang, Yangxin, Qichun, Dazhi, Jiayu, Huangpi, Xianning, Songzi, Macheng, Jingshan, and Zhijiang, for a total of thirteen counties. The third-class disaster areas are Anlu, Gongan, Zhongxiang, Puqi, and Jingmen, for a total of five counties. The fourth-class disaster areas are Suixian, Yunxian, Dangyang, Yidu, Chongyang, Luotian, Changyang, Gucheng, Nanzhang, and Xiangyang, for a total of ten counties. There are more than 10 million victims, and the relief funds received from various parties are still very small. The Hubei branch of the National Flood Relief Committee has received 50,000 yuan from consultant Baker, 100,000 US dollars from the American Red Cross, and 3,000 Japanese yen from the Japanese Disaster Relief Sympathy Association. The Hubei Flood Disaster Relief Association has received 170,000 yuan from the Central Government, 100,000 yuan from Guangdong merchants, and 50,000 yuan from the Hankou banking industry, as well as donations from individuals, totaling less than one million yuan. After issuing 5,000 yuan to the counties with the most serious disasters, the remaining counties still feel disappointed. The Relief Branch believes that the relief funds are too small to be of much help, so it telegraphed Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance on the 9th, requesting him to quickly allocate huge funds for relief efforts. The Emergency Relief Association has also sent letters to people from other provinces in Hankou, asking them to send telegrams to their respective provinces to raise funds. There is no shortage of charitable people in the country, and hearing of the severe disaster in Hubei, they will surely be happy to contribute. As for the relief organizations, the earliest established organization is the Hubei Flood Disaster Relief Association, jointly organized by all sectors of the party, government, military, and commerce. The next is the Hubei Branch of the Flood Relief Association, jointly organized by all sectors of Chinese and foreign countries. Recently, for the convenience of handling affairs, it has been decided to divide the authority. The Hubei Branch will be responsible for the Hankou emergency relief matters, and the Emergency Relief Association and the Hubei Branch will be jointly responsible for the emergency relief in various counties. In reality, they will still maintain contact. In addition, there are also the Central Health Group's Office in Hankou, the North China Disaster Relief Association, the Northeastern Four Provinces Charitable Federation, the Universal Moral Society, the Chinese Jisheng Society, and the World Red Cross Society China Headquarters Relief Team, which jointly organized a relief team. The first team, led by Yang Zigong, chairman of the Northeastern Four Provinces Charitable Federation, departed for Xindi on the 7th. The second team, led by Du Yannian, director of the National Flood Relief Committee's office in Hubei disaster area, is scheduled to depart for Fankou on the 10th to handle emergency relief matters. It is said that Mr. Zhu Qinglan will be in charge of the labor relief projects. (September 9th)

Hankou Headquarters to Try Wang Junjie 68

Will be Sentenced for the Crime of Murdering His Superior Officer

And Issue an Order to Assist in the Arrest of Accomplices

Hankou News: He Zhenfan, the acting division commander of the 34th Division, was killed by Wang Junjie, the brigade commander of the division, in Xiantao. The Wuhan Headquarters has lured Wang to Hankou and arrested him on August 2nd. It has also organized a military tribunal, with Xu Yuanquan, the bandit suppression commissioner of the Sichuan-Hunan-Hubei border area, as the presiding judge, and Ye Peng, the chief of staff of the garrison headquarters, as the judge, to conduct the trial and determine the sentence in order to uphold the law. After the tribunal was established, Xu Yuanquan personally brought Wang Junjie, Zhao Jizhi, Yao Yingcheng, and others to trial. Later, because Xu left to suppress bandits, Judge Ye Peng continued to question them. Through various methods, the truth of the case was clarified. Wang will be sentenced for the crime of murdering his superior officer. According to the Garrison Headquarters, Ye is currently drafting the sentence, which will be announced within a few days. Among the accomplices, Hu Shufu, Li Xiuzhi, and Yuan Youlong are still at large. Yesterday, the Headquarters issued an order to all troops to assist in their arrest. The order stated: It has been ordered that Wang Junjie, the brigade commander of the 34th Division, be dismissed and taken into custody. His accomplices Hu Shufu, Li Xiuzhi, and Yuan Youlong are definitely accomplices. The acting division commander of the division, Zhang Wanxin, was secretly ordered to escort them to Hankou for trial. After the acting division commander replied, stating that he would comply with the order, the suspects had fled for fear of punishment. People have been sent out to search for them for days, but they have not been caught. In addition to ordering a strict search, we request all agencies and troops to assist in the arrest to avoid any escapees. In addition to replying by telegram and issuing separate orders, we hereby order you to comply with the order and instruct your subordinates to assist in the arrest. (September 9th)

The Zhu Shude Case: Bullet Recovered 69

Jinan Correspondence: Since the Zhu Shude case occurred on July 27th, over forty days have passed. The most important piece of evidence in the case, the murder bullet, remained undiscovered for a long time. It was only today (the 8th) that Wang Weijun found it, which must be considered a significant discovery. On the day of the incident, Local Court Prosecutor Li Wenzhai went to the scene for inspection that very evening. The next day, Prosecutor Liu Rongshan also went for inspection, but both failed to find the bullet's location. After the deceased was placed in a coffin, the local constable, Wang Yuan, found the bullet casing under the east window of the west room. Since then, Zhu’s younger sister, Shuxin, repeatedly stated to the court that since the bullet could not be found in the room where Zhu Shude tragically died, she would not accept the suicide theory. Prosecutor Liu Rongshan, on the 21st of last month, also brought judicial police to Wang Weijun’s house, to the room where Zhu Shude tragically died, for a detailed search. However, nothing was found on the walls or the ground. On the 27th of last month, the Local Court Prosecutor's Office filed a public prosecution, accusing Wang Weijun and Liu Hesheng (Wang's wife) of concealing military firearms and assisting in suicide. Zhu's younger sister, Shuxin, was still not satisfied and insisted on inspecting Wang Weijun's other rooms for traces of bullets. If a bullet could be found in another room, it would undoubtedly prove that it was a brutal murder and the body was moved. Around 10:00 AM today, the court dispatched Chief Judicial Police Officer Xi Linge, Zhu's family representative Zhu Xifang, and brought the defendant Wang Weijun from the detention center, along with four judicial police officers, to Wang's residence for another inspection. Yang Yichao, a patrol officer from the relevant Public Security Bureau, also arrived, along with Wang Weijun's father, Wang Jinghai. They all went to the south room of the west house. The room was covered in cobwebs and dust, and cluttered with various items. The bed where Zhu Shude slept had been moved out, but the writing desk and bookshelves were still in place, with books neatly arranged. Everyone carefully searched the walls and the ground. After a while, Wang Weijun went to the northwest corner of the room and called Chief Judicial Police Officer Xi Linge and Patrol Officer Yang Yichao to point out a small hole in the paper pasted on the northwest corner seam, about three fen high and two and a half fen wide, appearing to be a bullet hole. With the consent of Zhu's family representative, Zhu Xifang, Wang's coachman was asked to find an axe to further examine the area. The soil on the wall was very loose, and the bullet did not penetrate deeply, as it was blocked by a stone. The bullet was found inside. It was immediately taken out for examination. The bullet was six or seven fen high and five or six fen thick, brand new, with a flat bullet head. Based on measurements, the bullet hole was three chi three cun above the ground and penetrated one cun seven fen into the wall. According to Wang Weijun, based on the direction and height of the bullet hole, Zhu Shude must have been sitting on the bed against the west wall, using her left hand to shoot herself. The flat bullet head was due to hitting a stone inside the wall. Chief Judicial Police Officer Xi Linge said that if Zhu Shude shot herself while sitting on the bed, the mosquito net on the bed should also have bullet holes and should be found and compared. Wang Weijun said that the mosquito net was already gone. Xi Linge then called Court President Hu Ji to report. The court then sent Judge Li Hongye to investigate. During this time, everyone went to the north room (Wang Weijun's living room) to inspect. Zhu's family representative Zhu Xifang started to flip through the paintings on the wall, and Wang Weijun became furious, almost leading to a quarrel. At around 12:30 PM, Judge Li Hongye arrived, and they went to the south room of the west house for another inspection, examining the bullet closely. He instructed the judicial police that the investigation of evidence should not be made public today, and that anyone not related to the case should leave immediately. He then questioned Wang Weijun about the whereabouts of the mosquito net. Wang replied that the mosquito net was given to the local constable Wang Yuan, and the bed had been sold. The judge then ordered Wang Yuan to be summoned for questioning. Wang Yuan flatly denied it. When Wang Weijun was questioned again, he lowered his head and remained silent. The judge ordered a return to the court for further trial and called Jieqing Photography Studio by phone to take several photos of the bullet hole in the west room. At the same time, bloodstains were found on the bricks on the ground outside the west room. The judge ordered the police officers to dig up the bricks, wrap them in paper, and take them back to the court along with the bullet. At 2:30 PM, the group returned to the court by car, and Wang Weijun was taken back to the detention center for further detention. (September 8th)

Guangdong Province Bans Refusal to Use Old Silver Coins 70

Official-Business Conference Decides on Two Prohibition Measures

Execution of Penalties to Begin on September 15th

Guangzhou Correspondence: The currency system of Guangdong Province originally uniformly circulated twenty-cent silver coins. However, silver merchants took the opportunity to create new and old coin distinctions to make huge profits. Government-minted silver coins naturally have chronological differences, but in terms of purity, coins minted at different times all adhere to the regulations and are no different. However, silver merchants have consistently based the value of new and old coins on their age, using new coins at face value and discounting old coins. Recently, this practice has become increasingly rampant, with old coins being discounted as low as 93 or 94 percent. Small merchants often suffer invisible losses in their transactions. They have repeatedly appealed to the authorities to find ways to maintain the value of the coins. Yesterday, the financial authorities convened representatives from various businesses to discuss methods of maintaining the currency's value. Those present at the meeting included representatives from the Silver Industry Zhongxin Hall, the Silver Industry Association, the City Chamber of Commerce, the Central Bank, and the Department of Finance, totaling more than ten people. The meeting concluded with a unanimous decision to strictly prohibit the discounting of old coins. The prohibition measures discussed are as follows: (1) The Department of Finance will rename the Guangdong Province Coin Appraisal Committee to the Coin Appraisal Committee, effective from September 15th. All revenue and expenditures of public and private organizations in the province shall be based on full-weight official coins, regardless of their age. Violations will be subject to the penalties outlined in Articles 9 and 10 of the appraisal regulations approved by the Department of Finance. Article 9 states that if any store refuses to accept old coins, they will be fined fifty yuan by the appraisal committee upon confirmation of the report. Article 10 states that if personnel of government tax collection agencies refuse to accept full-weight official old coins, merchants may send the rejected coins to the committee for appraisal. Upon confirmation, the committee will submit a report to the Department of Finance, which will issue orders to the respective supervisory authorities to dismiss the offending official as a warning. If it is a store, the committee may submit a report to the Department of Finance to revoke its business license and order it to close. (2) The monthly expenses of the Coin Appraisal Committee were originally shared by the Central Bank, the City Chamber of Commerce, and various businesses. The Central Bank and the City Chamber of Commerce have recently sent letters requesting to discontinue their contributions. It has now been decided that the Department of Finance will send separate letters to the Central Bank and the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting them to continue contributing according to the original amounts. After the above two proposals were passed, the meeting adjourned. It is reported that the Department of Finance has decided to implement the penalties on September 15th. If anyone dares to discriminate against old coins again, the Department of Finance will summon the merchant for a warning upon discovery. Subsequent offenses will be punished according to regulations, and a third violation will result in a closure order as a warning. At the same time, the Department of Finance has sent separate letters to the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, ordering the police to notify them to immediately arrest and severely punish those who refuse to issue receipts for silver transactions and use this as a means to coerce and refuse to accept old coins. (September 5th)

Zhejiang Province Rectifies Defense Corps in Various Counties 71

All Organizations Must Be Established Before the 20th of This Month

The Security Department of the Zhejiang Provincial Government has formulated procedures and measures for rectifying the defense corps and eliminating bandits and communists. Recently, the department found that the organization of the defense corps in various counties was complex and the structures varied greatly. Many of the corps members were recruited from undesirable elements, resulting in a weak sense of responsibility and poor self-defense capabilities. In fact, not only were they unable to suppress bandits, but they were often exploited by them. Therefore, it was decided to rectify the defense corps, and it was proposed to change the corps members to a mix of voluntary and hired personnel. Last month, a military training program for defense corps was held, with a total of 240 trainees. They have now graduated and been assigned to various counties to provide on-site training to the defense corps in their respective counties. The provincial government has ordered that the defense corps in all counties be established before the 20th of this month so that all counties can have self-defense capabilities to assist the security teams. It is reported that Zhu Mingtao, the director of the Security Department, plans to personally visit Jiangshan, Changshan, Kaihua, and other counties bordering Zhejiang, Fujian, and Jiangxi in the latter half of this month to inspect the defenses and instruct the county magistrates and corps leaders on the proper measures.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 72

The Whole Story of the Water Patrol Causing Trouble in a Neighboring County: Chen A'gen, a second-class water patrol officer of the Second Team of the Water Patrol Corps of Jinshan County, gathered his colleagues in plain clothes last night (the 8th) at around 11:00 PM and beat a woman named Xu Qian from Xiuye Bridge Beach. Each household, hearing the woman's cries for help in their sleep, came out to investigate. It was learned that the woman was from the Cuanlai Temple and was returning from pilgrimage to the Nihe Beach, temporarily docked here waiting for the tide. The men on the boat had gone ashore for tea, and the seven women on the boat had fallen asleep. Suddenly, two men in gray uniforms and plain clothes, holding electric lights, boarded the boat claiming to inspect it. They turned unreasonable, searched without justification, slapped faces, and kicked feet, hence the cries for help. A shop assistant first apprehended Chen Gensheng, the water patrol officer who caused the trouble, while the two men in plain clothes took the opportunity to escape. The police station of the Third Branch was notified by telegram and dispatched police to bring both parties to the county Public Security Bureau for investigation. According to Chen A'gen, he was escorting Team Leader Tan to Songjiang and was informed that there were many suspicious incense boats, so he went to search them. The woman then started shouting wildly, but he did not actually beat her. Later, Team Leader Tan went to the bureau to apologize and punished the water patrol officer with twenty lashes before taking him back to be dealt with according to the law. However, it is reported that the Public Security Bureau has transferred this case to the County Court for handling.

The Zhou Family in Fenwutou Village Suffers a Burglary: Zhou Jin's family, residents of Fenwutou Village in Fengjing Township, were suddenly attacked by seven or eight bandits around 8:00 PM the day before yesterday. They spoke in mixed accents, held long guns, and fired two shots in the air as a warning before entering the house to loot. Clothing and silver dollars worth hundreds of yuan were stolen. After the robbery, they left in a swaggering manner.

Qingpu 73

A Kidnapping Case Occurs in Chelu Village: The Shen family in Chelu Village, Second District of the county, were suddenly attacked by nine bandits armed with weapons the night before last. Two brothers were kidnapped, and a ransom of eight thousand yuan was demanded. The Shen family sent someone to negotiate, and the bandits demanded at least five thousand yuan. Currently, the Shen family is unable to raise the ransom and is still being held in the bandits' den. What Does Free Marriage Have to Do With an Aunt? Ye Xue'e, the daughter of Ye, who lives in the county seat on Qian Street, is in her early twenties and unmarried. She graduated from the Dongya Sports Academy and worked in Guangdong last year. She met a man named Chen and fell in love at first sight, wishing to make a lifelong commitment. The woman also obtained her mother's consent, but when relatives found out, they strongly opposed it, claiming it would disgrace the family. This time, Xue'e returned home for business and was insulted and beaten by her aunt, resulting in injuries all over her body. Afterward, she filed a complaint with the county government for examination and punishment according to the law and requested assistance from the county party headquarters.

Kunshan 74

A Robbery Case Occurs Outside the North Gate: The home of Qiu Guoying, a Hunanese resident living outside the North Gate near the Xu Riverbank, was suddenly attacked by a bandit boat at around 2:00 AM on the 8th. Multiple bandits speaking the Jiangbei dialect disembarked, entered Qiu's house, and tied up the men, women, and children. They then looted everything. Before leaving, they stole over three hundred ducks raised by Qiu. Afterward, Qiu filed a report with the county government requesting a strict investigation.

Nantong 75

Refugees from Xinghua Arrive in Tongzhou: The Xinghua Relief Group, together with the Xinghua County Government, used the Rui Da Wheel to transport 301 refugees to Tongzhou. On the 9th, they sailed to the west of the city. Over 100 of them volunteered to go to Shanghai and were sent to Tianshenggang to board a downstream riverboat for departure. The rest were all left at the nursing home and shelter.

Three Counties Jointly Manage the Sandbar Embankment Rescue: After last month's high tide, the Liu Hai Sandbar Embankment suffered many collapses. The Construction Department has ordered Nantong, Jiangyin, and Changshu, the three counties that jointly administer the island, to jointly rush to carry out the embankment rescue project. The estimated cost is 15,000 yuan, which will be temporarily borrowed from the beneficiary households based on the standard of cultivated land. This loan will be offset by the mou tax.

Accounting Is Busy, Clearing Up Old Habits and Thoroughly Eliminating Malpractices: In the case of irregularities in the collection of taxes in Tongzhou, it has now been decided to conduct an annual accounting to determine whether it is consistent with the amount submitted. On the 9th, the county government sent Zhu Ziruo and others involved in the case to the Department of Finance under police escort. At the same time, collection officers were dispatched to the province to be interrogated, so that the truth of the malpractices could be thoroughly understood.

Wuxi 76

Reply to the Letter on the Date of Commencement of Business Tax Collection: After the Bureau consulted with the Chamber of Commerce and invited various industries to make separate identifications of the Wuxi business tax, the first quarter's tax silver has been remitted. Director Wang received instructions from the Department of Finance yesterday, which required that the summer tax be collected and reported by September 10, regardless of whether the households were fully identified or had outstanding balances. The amount of tax collected was to be reported in a report form and sent to the Department for verification, and preparations were to be made for the autumn tax collection as soon as possible. Director Wang immediately forwarded the letter to the Chamber of Commerce. The County Chamber of Commerce responded that the date of commencement of business tax collection was previously discussed with County Magistrate Pan and former Director Yang Wubian when they went to Zhenjiang to negotiate. The Department of Finance insisted that Zhenjiang had already recognized it and respected the Provincial Government's resolution, and the collection was commenced on April 1. The Qian industry also had Chairman Lu Xiaobo of the Chamber of Commerce take the lead in paying the first quarter's tax, considering the overall situation. The final result was that after returning to Wuxi, the Business Tax Bureau would notify various industries to pay the first quarter's tax first. When the stamp was issued, the month was not temporarily indicated, and the case would be handled in accordance with the general case after the whole province decided on the plan. The Provincial Magistrate Pan had reported the details of the negotiation to the Provincial Government on record. At present, there are still many counties in Jiangsu Province that have not decided on the business tax, and for the date of commencement of collection, since the business tax was implemented by the Chamber of Commerce in June, many people preferred to clear the fiscal year of the 19th year and start from the autumn. Considering the situation in Wuxi, the silkworm crop failed this year, followed by the flood, and the market was depressed. The business tax was actually paid in the autumn. If only one quarter was collected, and then another autumn tax had to be collected, it would be impossible to do so in fact. The above information has been replied to the Business Tax Bureau.

Over 280,000 Mou of Farmland Affected by the Disaster: The County Government previously received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs to investigate and report the actual situation of the disaster in the county so as to compile the information. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Chen filled out a form yesterday and reported the actual situation of the disaster in the county. The total population of the entire county was 194,793 households, or 944,544 people, and the number of farmers affected by the disaster was about 128,000. The total area of agricultural land that was completely destroyed and hopeless was 287,834 mou, 8 fen, 8 li, and 8 hao. As for those that were not submerged, judging from the current situation, if there is no wind or rain, a medium harvest can be expected. The county's crops have always been 80% rice and 20% mulberry. This time, in addition to the rice fields being flooded, many mulberry trees were also submerged. Not only are the mulberry leaves yellowed now, making it difficult to raise autumn silkworms, but also the roots of the mulberry trees have been damaged, and the spring silkworm crop next year will also be affected.

Strictly Prohibit the Performance of Southern Opera: The second party-government meeting in the county was held at the county government yesterday, chaired by County Magistrate Chen Chuande. The important cases decided are as follows: 1. The County Government proposed that the organization of people's organizations should comply with the provisions of the revised organizational plan of the people's organizations regarding the procedure. It was decided to pass it. 2. The County Executive Committee proposed that Southern Opera, which affects social morals, has long been prohibited. If there are still performances in the future, they should be strictly arrested and punished. 3. The County Supervisory Committee proposed that Tan Huang Opera, mythological martial arts novels, and mythological movies have a great impact on social morals and should be strictly prohibited by both the party and the government. The above two items were discussed together and decided as follows: A. In the future, if there are Southern Opera performances that are related to social morals, or similar Tan Huang performances, the Public Security Bureau will investigate and strictly prohibit them. Violators will be arrested and prosecuted. B. Obscene mythological martial arts novels will be investigated and strictly prohibited by the County Party Headquarters, the Education Bureau, and the Public Security Bureau. C. The screening of film films will be handled by the Education Bureau from September 15th, in accordance with the results of the review of the Central Film Review Committee and the regulations. 4. The County Supervisory Committee proposed that the party headquarters recently joined forces with various theaters to raise funds for disaster relief, and the Public Security Bureau should notify its subordinates to assist at any time. It was decided to pass it. 5. The County Supervisory Committee proposed that the construction of various theaters and entertainment venues in the future should be carefully investigated by the Construction Bureau to avoid further misfortune. It was decided to pass it. 6. The plan to reorganize the county's water conservancy has not yet been implemented. A water conservancy research association should be established to discuss and implement the plan. It was decided that the county government would investigate and quickly establish a water conservancy research association to discuss and proceed.

The Price of Autumn Silkworm Cocoons Is Ninety Yuan Per Load: The silk factories in the county have received relief bonds and are starting their machines to provide a livelihood for female workers. Therefore, they are renting cocoon shops and buying autumn cocoons one after another. In the past three or four days, 124 people have reported to the cocoon industry association for opening cocoons as of yesterday, and there are still more reporting. The scene is no less lively than the spring cocoon season. The early cocoon shops in the four villages have been weighed for three or four days. The market price of autumn cocoons in the past few days has been 60 to 70 yuan per load. Yesterday, the price in Beiqiao Jixiangbang and other places was released to 80 yuan. Gongtailong in Shitou, Yingyi in Chang'an Bridge, and Xingchang in Gu Ting Temple have all started weighing one after another, with a market price of 60 yuan. Yesterday, the price of each line was mutually released to 90 yuan per load, but there were few goods. The current silk market is actually losing money in the competition for cocoons. The drying loss of autumn cocoons is about 280 catties, and the reeling loss is about 580 catties.

Changzhou 77

A Robbery and Injury Occurs Near Xixia: The home of Wang Fuchu in Putang Village near Xixia Town in Wu County was suddenly attacked by dozens of armed bandits at around 2:00 AM on the 8th. They broke into the house and looted. After searching for silver dollars and clothing, they still thought it was not enough. They tied up Wang Fuchu and his grandson Hao Kang and burned them with fire to force them to tell where the silver was hidden. Finally, they packed up the stolen goods and left with a roar. It is said that Fuchu is 64 years old and has serious injuries. He is being treated. Villagers on the Way to Pay Grain Were Robbed: At about 1:00 PM the day before yesterday, villagers Bian Dabao, Po Fuhai, and Wei Renbao from Gujiatang Village in the northern countryside of Wu County were robbed on their way to the city to pay grain. Two bandits, each holding a box gun, stepped forward to rob them. Dozens of yuan of silver dollars and land deeds were stolen from Bian and others. On the 9th, the nearby Public Security Bureau reported the case to the city and asked for an arrest.

Request to Postpone the Imposition of Survey Fees: Wu County was ordered to collect a survey fee of one jiao per mou. The County Party Headquarters and the district chiefs of various districts believed that this imposition exceeded the regulation of one percent of the land price, and the silkworm and wheat harvests this year were poor, and the autumn harvest was hopeless. On the 9th, they telegraphed the province to request permission to temporarily postpone the imposition in order to alleviate the people's difficulties.

Yangzhou 78

Sheltering Refugees and Handling Relief Plans: As of 10:00 AM on the 9th, a total of 3,500 refugees have been sheltered in the county. In Gaoyou, there are still a large number of refugees, about 5,000, being transported south one after another. Mr. Ma Jing'ang, the representative of the county, reported to the Disaster Relief Federation and requested that a way be found to shelter them. The Provincial Righteous Relief Association also sent a telegram stating that the Public Security Bureau should be entrusted to find more shelters. As for the relief work, the representatives of the refugees in the Second District, Nanguang, Liu Shizong and Xu Chunyang, and others, and the representatives of the towns and villages in the Yong'an Town, Zhang Hanzhang, and others, and the towns and villages in the Seventh District, Qiaoshu, Dinggou, Dingjiahuo, Yanhuang, Shaoshui, Zhou Hantang, and others, said that the water was five or six feet deep and the relief supplies could not reach them from Shaobo. The representatives were sent to Yangzhou to set up a flood relief association and requested relief personnel to distribute the relief from Xiannv Temple, Dahan, directly to the two flood relief offices in Qiaoshu and Dinggou. On the 9th, the urgent relief association telegraphed Sun Zhongying in Tianjin, asking him to raise funds and to encourage the fundraising committee members Wang Jingting, Zhu Gan臣, Tang Ewu, and Song Shenzhi to depart from Yangzhou to Beijing and Shanghai to work hard.

Rugao 79

A Large Number of Refugees Rescued and Transported to Rugao: The Rugao Reception Committee for Disaster-Stricken People Transported Along the Canal sent several civilian ships to rescue refugees in Dongtai and other places. At 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon, 371 disaster-stricken people were transported from Dongtai and immediately sent to various disaster-stricken people's shelters. It is said that they are all from Xiyuan Xiaohai and other districts in Dongtai County. When the water level was high in those places, it reached the roofs of the houses, and at least to the chest. About 20% of those who did not escape were drowned. The reporter spoke with them, and the refugees said with tears in their eyes, "It's so tragic."

Gaoyou 80

A Kidnapping and Robbery Occurs in Gaoganduo: At about 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, six awning boats suddenly arrived at Nanganduo in the county. Thirty or forty bandits, each carrying guns, swarmed ashore and searched house to house. Before leaving, they kidnapped eight farmers, men and women, including the Zhou, Chen, and Yang families.

Huzhou 81

Recent News on Flood Relief: The Wuxing Flood Relief Committee was established last month and established branch offices in each district, and issued flood survey forms to each village and neighborhood committee, setting a deadline for detailed investigation of the disaster situation and the number of disaster victims in order to distribute relief accordingly. As for raising relief funds, wealthy gentry and merchants in Nanxun have jointly raised 50,000 yuan, half of which will be retained in Xun for self-distribution, and the remaining 25,000 yuan will be allocated to the county relief fund first. In recent days, County Magistrate Li has personally gone to the countryside with gentry and merchants who are familiar with each district to solicit donations and has reportedly raised 10,000 yuan. Together with the 30,000 yuan from the National Government, 30,000 yuan from the Zhejiang Provincial Government, 3,000 yuan from the Zhejiang Relief Association, and various donations from compatriots in Shanghai, the total has reached more than 100,000 yuan. Once the disaster survey forms from each district have been collected and calculated, the relief will be distributed immediately. The farmers in Jingshan Daitou, Xia'ang, Nan Shuanglin, and other places, who were impatient and could not wait any longer, engaged in riots. The Flood Relief Committee sent people to the countryside to persuade them and explain the recent fundraising situation and relief distribution methods of the Flood Relief Association, so that they all calmed down and nothing happened.

Pinghu 82

District Chief Incites Military Mutiny and Is Accused: Because the district chief of the Fourth District (Xincang) of Pinghu, Zhu Chenguang, in the sixth lunar month, under the pretext of rewarding the 16th Transport Team of the Provincial Security Team stationed in the town, raised funds from the local area, but Zhu privately deducted half of the funds. When the garrison learned about it, it incited a military mutiny, causing harm to the local area. Zhu was the real culprit and was accused of it to the Department of Civil Affairs. It is reported that the Department of Civil Affairs has instructed the county government to thoroughly investigate. After receiving the order, the county government ordered the district chief of the First District, Chen Kai, and the roving assistant Shen Canru to investigate and verify.

Bee Incident: Farmers Demand Compensation: After the farmers requested the county government to move out of the Han Family Temple East Italian Bee Farm, the turmoil subsided. Recently, it has been reported that the farmers have suffered considerable losses due to the bee damage to the crops and have to demand compensation in order to maintain their livelihood. On the 8th, they properly discussed the method with the farmers' association and requested assistance from the County Party Headquarters and petitioned the county government for compensation. However, the bee farm believes that bees are beneficial and harmless to rice and is unwilling to suffer this fate. Ningbo 83

Yao City's One Night of False Alarm: Rumors suddenly spread in Yao City last night that bandits were going to rob money houses. For a time, the people of Yao City were all panicked. The Second Battalion Headquarters of the Security Team and the Public Security Bureau declared martial law that night and sent police to patrol the city gates. Fortunately, nothing happened until dawn. It is said that there are two reasons for the origin of the rumors. One is that the Heyuan Money House in the city had a dispute with a customer over interest, causing a big conflict. The money house then sent a telegram to the military and police to report it and asked them to arrest people. The second is that the members of the leather workers' association caused a dispute because of the collection of membership fees. Later, the trade union reported to the military and police agencies that there were reactionaries. At about 6:00 PM that afternoon, armed military police arrested a bag craftsman at the Shuimenkou and two others in front of the Shao Family Garden, which led to the spread of rumors that bandits were robbing, causing the people of Yao City to suffer a night of false alarm.

Anqing 84

Educational Funding Relief Measures for Various Counties: The Provincial Education Department presented the educational funding relief measures for various counties in Anhui Province affected by the floods at the Provincial Government's regular meeting on the 4th. These measures were approved and resolved as follows: (1) The total county educational expenditure for the 20th year (of the Republic) shall not exceed the income for that year; (2) Administrative expenses shall be reduced, and the county shall submit proposals to the Education Department for approval to consolidate or abolish newly established institutions; (3) Regular expenses shall be prioritized for allocation, while temporary expenses shall be deferred; (4) Primary school buildings that have been flooded shall temporarily suspend classes, and students shall be assigned to nearby primary schools; (5) Primary schools that have not been flooded may expand their student enrollment; primary schools in urban areas may expand each grade to 50 students, while primary schools in rural areas shall have no fewer than 30 students per grade, adopting a combination or two-part system; if neighboring schools can be merged, they should be merged; (6) Subsidies and incentive allowances for all public and private schools may be reduced or suspended; (7) Existing old debts that were designated to be repaid within the 20th year shall be deferred to the next year for payment; (8) Those who have already prepared the budget for the 20th year shall re-prepare a statement of estimated actual income and expenditure for the 20th year, along with an explanatory report, and submit it to the Education Department; those who have not prepared a budget shall do the same; (9) These regulations shall not apply to counties that have not been affected by the disaster or counties where the disaster has not affected educational funding; (10) These measures shall be implemented by order of the Provincial Government through the Education Department.

Letter to the Editor

Letter from the Langxi Flood Relief Association 85

Having recently read the section on domestic news in your esteemed newspaper on the 25th, concerning the disaster assessment in Anhui Province, we find it inconsistent with the facts. According to our information, no disaster assessment personnel from Anhui, such as Hong Huichen and Chen Zhiding, visited Langxi to conduct an assessment. Instead, they made an arbitrary judgment based on the assumption that the disaster situation was relatively mild, which is greatly mistaken. Langxi is located downstream of Guangde and upstream of Wuhu. This year's flood was not only large but also sudden, caused by the backflow of the Yangtze River. The embanked fields were completely destroyed, and no seeds or grains remain. The disaster situation is extremely severe, unprecedented in history. Rice, grain, goods, houses, and livestock were all swept away. Tens of thousands of disaster victims are without clothing, food, or homes, standing and lying in the wind and rain for more than ten days and nights. To this day, the water has not receded, and deaths are piling up, beyond description. Previously, our association devised methods to provide relief, and the emergency relief office publicly appointed representatives to go to various places to seek aid for relief. Now, upon reading the aforementioned statement, we are extremely worried. In addition to sending telegrams to various relief agencies to clarify that the situation is not relatively mild and requesting the assessment personnel to come to Langxi for a personal assessment, we respectfully request the chief editor to publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section for correction, and we will be most grateful. Publicly declared by Zhu Tingliao and others, Chairmen of the Langxi County Flood Relief Association, Anhui, September 4th.

Shanghai Municipal Government Employees' Health Exercise Competition Schedule 95

Discussion on Postponement of National Games 96

Certain Central Committee Members and the Central Daily News Advocate for It

Nanjing, 11th – Local newspapers here have long reported that the National Games will be postponed to focus on disaster relief. However, the organizing committee has repeatedly corrected this. Today, the Central Daily News editorial on the issue of postponing the National Games concluded that matters have different scales of importance and urgency, and times have priorities and delays. Now, the disaster area has reached 16 provinces, and the number of disaster victims has reached 50 million. Comparing this with the National Games, what is the scale of importance and urgency? Since the newspaper represents the Central Government, the idea of postponing the National Games temporarily gains traction.

Nanjing, 10th – Central Telegram – The organizing committee has already denied the postponement of the National Games via public telegram. According to a certain Central Committee member, the flood is severe, and the National Government has explicitly ordered the cessation of all non-essential construction to concentrate financial resources on responding to the tragic disaster.

The National Games and its construction are certainly not as urgent as the life-and-death issue of millions of disaster victims. It is proposed to request the Central Government to postpone the event, stop all construction, and transfer funds for disaster relief. It is hoped that the sports community will consider the disaster victims and not insist on not postponing the event.

The Shanghai-Hong Kong-Tianjin Triangular Swimming Competition was held at the French Chamber of Commerce swimming pool last night at 9:15 PM. The pool is grand in scale and luxuriously decorated, unparalleled in Shanghai. That evening, the five-colored electric lights illuminated the pool, and the shimmering silver waves were picturesque. The music was loud and lively, enhancing people's interest. It was both pleasing to the eye and delightful to the ear. More than 700 men and women spectators felt as if they were in a crystal palace, happy and forgetting to return home. Chinese guests accounted for 40-50% of the audience. Mr. Shen Siliang, Honorary Director of the Association, was also invited as a distinguished guest. There were not many inter-port competition events. Since they were divided into three days, various performance programs were interspersed to provide variety. The performance results were all omitted. The competition ended at 12:00 AM.

Huang Zhenxing's Skills Amazed the Audience 100

Huang Zhenxing, a famous Chinese swimmer and the only middle-level athlete among the three teams from Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Tianjin, displayed excellent posture and strength in the water polo throw last night, surpassing all three teams. He threw three times in succession. The first throw was 66 feet 11 inches, the second throw was 70 feet 1 inch, and the third throw was 69 feet 6 inches. Every time he appeared, Chinese and Western guests in the audience applauded to welcome him. His amazing skill was such that he took the lead and stood out from the crowd. The people of Hong Kong were ecstatic, and the Chinese spectators were radiant.

As a result of the first day, Shanghai had 15 points, Hong Kong had 10 points, and Tianjin had 5 points. Shanghai's strength lay in the 100-yard breaststroke event, accounting for 8 points. Hong Kong was able to rank second, thanks to Huang Zhenxing's contribution.

No Football Match in Next Year's International Games 106

International Football Association Cables Reasons

China's Dispatch of a Football Team Will Be Just a Pipe Dream

Conflict in the Definition of Amateur Sports

The All-China Sports Federation intended to send a Chinese football team to participate in next year's World Games. However, since the published schedule of the World Games did not include a football competition, the Federation telegraphed the International Football Association in Amsterdam to inquire. Recently, a letter was received from Mr. He Qimen, honorary secretary of the Association, stating the following reasons, stating that the British-style football championship will be removed from the World Games to be held in the United States next year. The American Football Association had resolved at the Helson-Fas Conference in 1927 that if the World Games recognized the definition of amateur sports established by the Association, then football would be included in the World Games program. The two associations subsequently agreed, and the event was included in the 1928 World Games. The 1930 World Games conference in Berlin revised the definition of amateur sports. The International Football Association conference (1930) in Budapest and 1931 in Berlin, however, insisted on the Association's original definition. Since the two parties could not agree, it was decided not to include the international football competition in next year's World Games program.

(Note) Members of the International Football Association must be governed by the Association. The World Games cannot hold international football competitions on its own without the Association's permission.

Local News

Zhejiang Provincial Government Negotiates with Yongshun Steamship Company 124

Small Steamer Damages Embankment

Yongan Steamer Seized

Heavy Fine to Repair Dams

Inland river steamers, after the water receded slightly in the latter half of last month, resumed operations one after another. However, after a major flood occurred in Shaoyang, the steamers on the Suzhou-Wuxi-Changzhou-Kunshan routes were transferred to northern Jiangsu to transport refugees and were suspended again. In Shanghai, the Shanghai-Hangzhou, Shanghai-Suzhou, and Shanghai-Lake Tai routes could still operate normally. Unexpectedly, heavy rain resumed on the fifth of this month, lasting for three days and nights. The water that had receded in the interior of Jiangsu and Zhejiang rose again. The small steamers that had resumed operations were forced to stop due to the rising water. The Yongshun Steamship Company on the Shanghai-Lake Tai route violated the order and sailed, causing the embankment to be damaged. They were fined a huge sum of one hundred and twenty thousand yuan to be used for repairing the dams. This matter has not yet been resolved. Yesterday, reporters thoroughly investigated the situation from all sides. The details are as follows:

▲ Lake Tai Water Rises, Navigation Restricted: There are a total of six Shanghai-Huzhou steamers, which resumed operations in the latter half of last month, divided into morning and evening shifts. From the fifth of this month, heavy rain fell continuously for three days. The water level in Huzhou rose sharply, increasing by one foot and several inches. Huzhou has three large embankments, containing tens of thousands of acres of fields. Villagers, fearing that the embankments would be damaged by the water, prevented the steamers from sailing, and the county government also issued a notice prohibiting steamers from operating, in order to protect the embankments and avoid collapses and the flooding of farmland. The Farmers' Association also sent personnel to patrol and protect the area. All of the Shanghai-Lake Tai steamers stopped running after the fifth.

▲ Yongan Steamer Damages Embankment: One steamer was named Yongxin, and the other Yongan. They have great horsepower and are relatively fast. When the county government issued the ban on navigation, the company had not yet received the notice. Therefore, the Yongan steamer still departed from Shanghai. At that time, the water had risen sharply, and the waves generated by the ship were powerful, inevitably causing some damage to the embankment, loosening the soil. River water leaked into the farmland, and a section of the embankment was washed away by the water, causing an accident.

▲ Farmers' Association Requests Seizure of Steamer: After this incident occurred, the Huzhou Farmers' Association, on the grounds that Yongshun had violated the county government's ban and sailed during the flood, damaging the embankment and flooding farmland, reported the matter to both the county and provincial party departments, requesting the Zhejiang Provincial Government to severely punish the case and detain the company's steamer. The provincial government decided to approve the request and ordered the Huzhou County Government to first detain the Yongan steamer in Huzhou, prohibit it from operating, and prohibit the company's other steamers from sailing.

▲ Provincial Government Discusses Heavy Fine: The Zhejiang Provincial Government, after receiving the report, considered the commercial steamer's violation of the ban and the damage to the embankment during the flood to be a serious matter, different from accidental damage. It was brought up for discussion at the provincial affairs meeting. It was publicly decided that since the company's steamer had damaged the embankment, it should be ordered to repair it. After estimation, it was decided to fine the Yongshun Steamship Company 1.2 million yuan to be used for repairing the dams. The company will not be allowed to resume operations until the fine is paid, and the seized steamer will not be released.

▲ Steamship Company Tries to Intervene: The Yongshun Steamship Company has ordered the Yongxin steamer to also stop in Shanghai and not dare to sail. Meanwhile, it is trying to intervene from all sides, hoping to cancel the fine. However, the provincial government firmly refused. Later, Yongshun planned to abandon the Huzhou route and switch to the Shanghai-Xun route, but the Zhejiang Provincial Government also refused. This matter is currently being negotiated between the two parties, and it is not known how it will be resolved.

▲ Shanghai-Lake Tai Steamers All Stop: After this incident occurred, the Huzhou County Government has set up water level gauges in the nearby waterways. Small steamers will only be allowed to pass when the water level has dropped by one foot and two inches from the current level. Therefore, all Shanghai-Lake Tai steamers, such as those of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Yuantong Company, have all stopped running.

Yesterday's News on Disaster Relief in Various Provinces 125

City Boy Scouts to Collect Donations Along the Way Tomorrow

The Shanghai Boy Scout Flood Relief Donation Committee has decided to hold a city-wide Boy Scout disaster relief donation along the way tomorrow (the 12th). It has been approved by various party and government agencies. Thirty-two troops have joined, with approximately 2,000 Boy Scouts. They will all start collecting donations at their designated locations tomorrow morning at 6:00 a.m. and return to their troops at 2:00 a.m. It is reported that when collecting donations, the donations will be personally deposited by the donors into the donation box, and the Boy Scouts will give a commemorative card. White cards are for donations of two jiao or more, and yellow cards are for donations of one yuan or more. All troops of Boy Scouts plan to enter hotels, amusement parks, teahouses, restaurants, and other commercial places within their designated areas to collect donations. All expenses incurred by the Boy Scouts throughout the day will be borne by the Boy Scouts themselves. In order to facilitate the command of the city-wide Boy Scout donation, the office has borrowed the Moore Memorial Church on Sima Road (Nanjing Road) to facilitate the Boy Scouts' contact with all matters at any time. The donations collected must be submitted to the donation committee at that time. It is also scheduled to invite party and government agencies to the Moore Memorial Church on the morning of the 13th to supervise the opening of the funds.

Centralized Disaster Victim Shelter 126

Since the city's disaster victim shelter concentrated the disaster victims in the Chao Huishan Village behind the South Railway Station on Xiebopo Road on the 8th, the food distribution method has been changed. The various situations of the past two days are summarized as follows:

▲ Managing Meals: The shelter's office found it very difficult to manage meals when they were scattered in nine different locations. Therefore, they adopted the method of issuing steamed buns and cash. Since the centralization, they have hired people to manage meals, providing three meals a day like ordinary families. Each person is issued two bowls for use. However, the rice and vegetables are currently cooked separately, which is very cumbersome. It is rumored that they will adopt the method of pre-cooked rice and vegetables sold in the market in the future.

▲ Issuing Clothing and Bedding: The clothing and bedding that have been prepared include 1,000 sets of short shirts and pants, 800 quilts, 1,000 mats, 1,000 sets of cotton clothing, and 1,000 towels and soaps. It is planned to first issue each person a set of single clothing, a towel, and a soap within the day. Quilts and mats will also be issued in order. Because more and more disaster victims from northern Jiangsu have been arriving in Shanghai recently, it has been decided to add 500 sets of each type of clothing and bedding. The clothing donated from other sources will be issued after disinfection.

▲ Continuing Arrival of Disaster Victims: The arrival of disaster victims from Wuhan seems to have stopped. Therefore, the disaster victims who have continued to arrive in the past two days have all come from Shaobo, Gaoyou, and other places. It is estimated that more than 400 disaster victims arrived from Shaobo and Gaoyou at around 9 p.m. the night before last. Those who arrived yesterday morning included more than 100 people from Xinghua who landed at the Dada Wharf in the southern part of the city and more than 100 people from Gaoyou who arrived at the North Station by the Jinghu train. In total, more than 600 people arrived in the two days. After registration, they were all issued symbols. Because Chao Huishan Village could no longer accommodate them, they were housed in the Yongxi Hall in Xieqiao, the second shelter.

▲ Medical Statistics: Yesterday, Dr. Zhang Qunying of Shanghai Hospital announced that from August 30 to September 8, there were seven temporary clinics, 207 cases of dysentery, 72 cases of colds, 33 cases of enteritis, 136 cases of malaria, 21 cases of boils, 114 cases of enterocattarrh, 1 postpartum woman, 1 pregnant woman, 1 case of true cholera, and 1 death. In total, 717 people were treated in ten days, and five people (adults and children) died.

Minutes of the Meeting of the Emergency Relief Association for Water Disasters in Various Provinces 127

▲ Standing Committee Meeting: The Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for Water Disasters in Various Provinces held a Standing Committee meeting at 3 p.m. yesterday. The attendees included Xu Shiying, Wen Lant亭, Qu Wenliu, Huang Hanzhi, Yu Guanfu, Wu Zhihao, Zheng Yuxiu, Hu Xisheng, Qin Runqing, Pan Xulun, Zhang Zhijiang, Wang Xiaolai, Zhu Ziqiao, Hong Zhenjiu, Pan Gongzhan, Li Zuyu, Wu Yunzhai, Cui Xianlou, Xiang Songmao, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Ha Shaofu, Wang Yiting, Xu Yongzuo, Lu Bohong, etc. Xu Shiying chaired the meeting, and Mao Youfeng took the minutes. (A) Reporting Items: (1) Received a total of 189 documents; (2) Issued a total of 120 documents; (3) Received a total of 250,116.18 yuan in relief funds from the 2nd to the 8th, plus 1 yuan in lead money, 5 yuan in changed notes, 50 yuan in miscellaneous notes, and 15 yuan in counterfeit notes. Together with the previous receipts, the total relief funds received were 613,005.35 yuan, plus 200 taels of silver, 34 yuan in copper money, 39 yuan in foreign money, 5 yuan in changed notes, 50 yuan in miscellaneous notes, and 15 yuan in counterfeit notes. Of the above relief funds, 181,731.24 yuan was allocated for the first time and 186,952.35 yuan was allocated for the second time; (4) The current balance of relief funds is 244,321.76 yuan.
