▲ Mass Fundraising Conference: Yesterday, Mayor Zhang and others invited representatives of various trade associations in Shanghai to a dinner at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to discuss holding a fundraising conference. Representatives of more than 100 groups attended, with hundreds of people attending, and the atmosphere of enthusiastic disaster relief filled the venue for a while. The representatives of various trades all stated that this unprecedented flood was not only related to the survival of the country but also had a great impact on various industrial and commercial undertakings. They unanimously advocated convening meetings separately, starting to organize fundraising teams, and doing their best to raise funds for disaster relief, in order to achieve the goal of self-rescue and saving the country. During the dinner, Zhu Ziqiao reported on the disaster situation in the disaster area. Mayor Zhang and industry leaders Wu Zihao, Zhang Zilian, and Yin Jiefu all gave heartfelt speeches. Excerpts are as follows: Zhu Ziqiao reported, roughly saying, "Brothers, the disaster situation is particularly serious in Hankou, Gaoyou, and Shaobo. I personally took a plane to inspect the area. From the plane, I only saw the Yangtze River for thousands of miles, a vast expanse of water, with no trace of the banks. The treetops and rooftops floated on the surface of the water, as sparse as morning stars. Residents in the houses, the old and the weak, were all in the flood. Those who were fortunate enough to survive only escaped with their bare lives. In the places where disaster victims gathered, the sounds of crying for fathers, mothers, children, brothers, and sisters were heard from time to time. The situation was so tragic that it was heartbreaking. Passing through the Dongtai Taiyu area, there was nowhere that was not a watery country, and the number of deaths was countless. Therefore, we must do our best for emergency flood relief and must also dredge the Huai River, dredge the Yangtze River, and build embankments to prevent future disasters. Both symptomatic and fundamental treatments should be considered. I am willing to sacrifice everything and do my best from beginning to end. I hope that people from all walks of life will rise up and support me." Mayor Zhang said, roughly, "There are three essential elements for establishing a country: governance, food, land, and people. The lack of any one of these means that the country cannot be established. This time, the floods in various provinces, the land is submerged, and the people are suffering. Two of the three major elements have been harmed, which is a great loss to the country. The people of the whole country should unite their strength and go to the rescue together. During the European War, Germany had a slogan called 'National Mobilization,' which ordered the people of the whole country to defend the country. I think that this flood also requires the slogan of total mobilization and the power of total mobilization to save the great disaster," etc. Wu Zihao said, roughly, "Although various industries have successively risen to help with relief through business operations, it has not yet been universally implemented. Various industries must unite and work together and not lag behind others. This time, the clothing industry, regardless of labor and management, is willing to do its best for disaster relief. A few days ago, because we were acting on behalf of the State Council's Flood Relief Committee in handling 300,000 sets of cotton clothing, with the consent of both labor and management, the wage price was specially reduced. Each set was 1 jiao and 9 fen cheaper, for a total price reduction of 57,000 yuan," etc. Yin Jiefu reported, roughly, "Our clothing industry, in the name of the industry's trade union, has been soliciting donations from various trades and has decided that for seven days, 10% of the sales income of all trade stores in the city will be donated to disaster relief. As for the wholesale and forwarding stores, we have also done our best to solicit donations and have decided that each store will donate as much old cotton clothing printed in the current season as possible," Zhang Zilian said, roughly, "After the great floods in various provinces, the whole country has gathered its strength and is working hard to donate funds and handle emergency relief to save the affected compatriots. Now a large number of disaster victims have been rescued and transported to Shanghai, where the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has set up shelters to house them. Therefore, we compatriots who are fortunate enough not to have suffered should think about the disaster victims who have entered the shelters and not let the story of disaster victims crossing the border to eat big households repeat itself. Except for the old and weak, we must ensure that the strong have something to do and can support themselves. I am now willing to accept 100 disaster victims and house them in the various factories I run, train them, and let them work. If each factory can do this consistently, then it is also a smaller-scale work-for-relief method."

Zhang Zhijiang Telegraphed the Relief Situation in Northern Jiangsu 128

Zhang Zhijiang telegraphed to report that the disaster relief personnel in northern Jiangsu witnessed the disaster situation, saying that recently, the relief team, carrying relief supplies, set off by boat from Yangzhou to the disaster area and distributed them along the way. However, because the current was rapid at Liuzha, it was difficult for the small boat to move forward. When it reached Xiannv Temple, it hired more than a dozen civilian boats and towed them by boat to Kongjia Han and Maqiao. The water depth in each village was four or five feet, and the residents avoided climbing the high mounds, extending their necks to wait for rescue, which was unbearable to witness. The disaster situation in Gaofengqiao, Jijiayu Town, and other places was even more serious. About 2,000 disaster victims were gathered on the high mounds, and the houses and fields in the Qiaoyu Town Yangjia Village area were a vast expanse of water. About 5,000 to 6,000 disaster victims gathered on the high mounds and embankments or climbed on rooftops and branches to wait for rescue. About 4,000 disaster victims in Shefeng Embankment had gone without food for two or three days, and floating corpses were visible everywhere. After the relief supplies were distributed, the original boats were used to rescue the disaster victims who came to seek help. On the days of frugality, small boats and civilian boats transported relief personnel and drove to Shaobo Town, passing through Xinhiekou and Diaojiawan. The floodwater had receded, but the houses and houses were gone. Thousands of disaster victims were exposed to the wind and dew, and the situation was extremely miserable. The breach at Liuzha East was about 13 or 14 feet, and the water flowed inward in both places. Xinghua, Dongtai, and Qin counties in the lower reaches of the canal were all turned into swamps. The north and south breaches of Zongmaoshu Dawang Temple north of Liuzha were about four or five feet. The breach in the Shaobo earth dam washed away the lower dam, and the houses and fields were all submerged. Hundreds of disaster victims will be transported to Yangzhou and put into shelters. The relief workers reported that the Zhaoguan Dam on the Shaobo Canal bank had a breach of dozens of feet. The disaster victims were seen on the boat climbing on the branches, extending their necks to wait for rescue. The food they carried was distributed around, and the roofs of the houses in each town were completely submerged. An uncountable number of people drowned. After the wheat supplies were exhausted, they rushed back to transport food and coffins to save the living and the dead, etc. Sincerely reported, Zhang Zhijiang bowed.

Jiangsu Flood Relief Association News 129

▲ The Yangzhou Office Reported on Work:

A letter from Cao Songqiao and Yuan Xiaogu of the Yangzhou office of the association states that the work there is extremely tense. Since its establishment, Cao Hengru has transported rice to Huo Jiaqiao to distribute among dozens of villages, and Lu Shouchang has distributed supplies along the border of Taixian County. Yue Shen (Cao Songqiao) and Yan Jiyu, Liu Jifu, Wang Mubo, and others personally distributed supplies in the Shaobo area (a total of 48 villages and 80-90 settlements were supplied). Zhou Liangji went to Zaixing Village to supervise the construction of embankments, with funds allocated by the office. Ji Mei (Yuan Xiaogu) worked with Xu Houru, He Yengeng, Tang Zifeng, Ling Yaozeng, Huang Guoxiang, Ruan Yunzhong, Zhu Zhusun, Xu Tingsong, Yang Shengwu, Yang Jianong, Wang Liquan, Ding Xiaojiang, and others, some responsible for reception, some for investigation, some for liaison with various parties, and others divided into accounting, documentation, translation, and general affairs. They rise as early as 6 AM and retire as late as 1-2 AM every day. This matter is of great importance, with millions of disaster victims. The funds for reception, such as purchasing reed mats, preparing relief goods, and transportation, are enormous and all necessary, and not a single penny is spent recklessly. The association has only provided 25,000 yuan and 1,000 bags of flour, which is far from sufficient. Further assistance is earnestly requested. Initially, it was planned to focus on Jiangdu County, but after inspection, Jiangdu and Gaoyou counties have nearly one million people awaiting relief. Witnessing the urgency of the situation, it is impossible to stand idly by, so sometimes the scope of work is inevitably exceeded. Disaster relief is like fighting a fire, with no boundaries to divide, and there is no need to be restricted by county lines. As for urgent relief in Yangzhou, the county has repeatedly sent telegrams urging action, but the situation in Gaoyou cannot be delayed. Being unable to handle both simultaneously, it is hoped that other local gentry can be hired to take charge.

() The Xinghua Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai Appeals:

A letter was sent yesterday by the Xinghua Fellow-Provincials Association to the Xinghua community. It stated that the county has suffered from repeated famines and has not yet recovered. The great floods of the Republic Year 10 were followed by droughts and salinization in the 17th and 18th years. This year, in May, there were ten days of continuous heavy rain, and before the Huai River disaster occurred, the ditches were already full. When the three dams were opened simultaneously, the water depth on the plains reached ten feet. The farmers' year of hard work was entirely swept away. Furthermore, the water from the breach of the Gao-Shao dike and the three lakes flowed down the river, treating it as a ditch. When the water arrived, the people of Xinghua were still dreaming. Accompanied by fierce winds and torrential rain, the sound of crying shook the sky. The young and strong climbed trees and roofs, while the old and weak drifted with the current. Floating corpses were everywhere, and the floodwaters raged. As a result, Xinghua County, spanning over a hundred miles, was without a single piece of dry land. The county seat, the highest point, was half submerged, and countless houses outside the city were washed away. The breach has not been blocked to this day, and the water level continues to rise, day after day, month after month, threatening to submerge even this isolated city. The most tragic disaster this time is in Gaoyou and Shaobo, followed by Yancheng, Funing, Taidong, and Xinghua. Among the five counties of Yancheng, Xinghua is the most severely affected. Gaoyou and Xinghua share contiguous land, and Xinghua has the lowest terrain, receiving the earliest impact of the water. The ports to the sea have been blocked by wealthy merchants and reclamation companies, preventing drainage. Therefore, the water in Gaoyou and Shaobo may recede at times, but the water in Xinghua has no hope of drying up, and there is no time for cultivation. Those who have lost their homes and properties, it is clear, will either die from the water today or starve to death next year. Either they will die from waiting helplessly, or they will die from taking risks. The great disasters of the future are unimaginable. Your association is concerned about the suffering of the hungry and drowning. It is hoped that you will alleviate their suffering as soon as possible.

▲ Sending Personnel to Purchase Cotton Clothing:

The association believes that the weather is gradually cooling, and the disaster victims in various places lack clothing and bedding, fearing death from freezing. In addition to local procurement, advertisements were placed to solicit donations. In recent days, donations have been pouring in. Due to the widespread disaster and large population, it is still feared that it will be insufficient. Yesterday, staff member Wu Zhigang was sent to Suzhou to purchase supplies. It is heard that the association plans to pre-purchase 30,000 to 50,000 sets of cotton clothing and 10,000 to 20,000 quilts for distribution.

Qiao Baoyuan, the head of the Copper Mountain Emergency Relief effort for the association, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday despite his illness to discuss Copper Mountain affairs. The standing committee members, recognizing the heavy workload of the association and the difficulty for Director Cheng Jingsheng to leave the town for long, requested Qiao to return to town as a representative, while Cheng would stay in town to handle affairs, so as not to cause any delays. Qiao returned to town by train yesterday morning. The Copper Mountain Emergency Relief effort has already been initiated by Qiao's friend, Qiu Jinzhang, who was invited to conduct inspections. Director Qiao may need to visit for inspection after his health recovers.

Telegram Requesting the Opening of Salt Reclamation Dike 130

The Yangzhou Eight Counties Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai telegraphed the Provincial Government on the 9th, addressed to the Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Ye, and the Director of the Department of Construction, Sun. The telegram stated: We have received a telegram from the Zhenjiang-based Aftermath Relief Association for the Flood Disaster in Funing, Taidong, and Xinghua. It stated: According to a report from Shen Linsen, a refugee from Dongtai County, the east and west sides of the Dongtai Fan Dike are leaking, rendering it ineffective. The people of Dongtai claim that the disaster is due to companies such as Dafeng and Yuhua defying the provincial government's order to open up the ports to the sea. Now, the North-South, Middle, Mao-You Rivers, and Zi-Wu Rivers are nominally open, but in reality, they are blocked as before. For example, the lower reaches of the Xiaoyang River, newly dredged this year by Mr. Zhu Zhongjian of the Relief Association, are blocked by the Xiangfeng district, so that hundreds of miles of the old channel to the sea are surrounded by long dikes. This is the reason why this year's great flood has stagnated in the Yancheng, Funing, Taixing counties, making it difficult to drain. The director of the Dongtai County Public Security Bureau was ordered to open it, but it was blocked immediately after opening. It is unknown what role is being played in this. It seems necessary to appeal to your council to forward the request to the authorities and ask Zhang, the Pacification Commissioner, to personally supervise the opening of the long dike held by the company. Otherwise, not only will the massive amount of water in the lower counties be difficult to recede, but also Henan, Shandong, Anhui and Jiangsu will also be affected. In addition to having telegraphed the Jiangsu Construction Department in winter, please advocate for a consistent approach to save the disaster-stricken people. Upon reviewing the recent reports, it seems that the dredging of the waterway to the sea in the Dongtai area has been strictly enforced by your council, and a telegram has been sent to Pacification Commissioner Zhang to dispatch troops to Dongtai to suppress the situation. The eagerness to address the disaster and benefit the disaster victims is deeply appreciated. After discussion, it was decided that more than half of the disaster victims are in the five lower counties. If the accumulated water can be drained as soon as possible, not only will the displaced people be able to return to their homes and cultivate the land as soon as possible, but they can also plant wheat. This is indeed the fundamental plan for the current situation, which is more important than raising funds for relief. The companies are only concerned with protecting the small number of cotton fields within their dikes that have not been flooded. They are trying to deceive by citing the livelihoods of tenant farmers. Recently, the Huainan Salt Reclamation Association has come forward to argue by telegram, which is completely disregarding the overall situation. We believe that all belong to the same local area, and there should be no division in disaster relief and caring for the people. However, after careful consideration of the facts, weighing the priorities, how can we ignore this? Even if the livelihoods of a small number of reclamation farmers are slightly affected, other relief should be arranged separately. We cannot refrain from eating for fear of choking. We still hope that you will decisively and independently take charge and order the companies to dismantle all the dikes that obstruct the water from entering the sea, so as to facilitate drainage. Then the flood can be controlled, and the displaced people will have hope of survival. We respectfully submit this appeal with the utmost urgency. The Yangzhou Eight Counties Fellow-Provincials Association kowtows.

Investigation Report on Rush To Repair the Embankment Breach 131

People from various counties in the lower reaches of the river, which were flooded, gathered at Wu's residence on Xinzha Road yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM for an emergency meeting to discuss ways to urgently rescue their hometowns and to invite Mr. Shen Zhuowu to attend and report on the situation. Before Shen spoke, Chen Qintuan stood up and said that the counties of Gaoyou, Xinghua, Dongtai, Jiangdu, and Taixian had all become watery realms after the Yun Dike broke. The water had reached the rooftops. Requests were made to rush to repair the breach, but to no avail. The responsible personnel openly stated that there would be no action until the water receded. How could the compatriots in the counties floating on the water wait? Taking Xinghua County as an example, there were more than 500,000 people floating on the water waiting for rescue, in an extremely tragic situation. If they waited for the water to recede before repairing the breach, the flooded people would inevitably die completely. What a terrible event this would be! Now, Mr. Shen has acted bravely and is trying to find a way to rush to repair the breach. He asked all the fellow villagers to pay their respects and invited Mr. Shen to report on the situation. Shen Zhuowu reported that the damage caused by the breach of the Yun Dike in the lower counties was a complete loss for the entire Chinese nation. At the time of the breach, the priority was to rescue lives. At the same time, we must

Page 14

We should also focus on rushing to repair the breach, otherwise the water flow will not stop, and the disaster area will inevitably expand. It is especially important to understand the words of the sages: "A major flood in the lower reaches in one year means that there will inevitably be a major drought in the upper reaches for three years." Therefore, rushing to repair the breach is not only to save the lives of the people in the lower reaches, but also to prevent drought in the upper reaches. After the breach, I risked going to Shaobo to inspect and found that the work to repair the Black Fish Pond breach was quite slow, and the effectiveness was uncertain. Labor and money were wasted, and time was wasted, causing trouble. I was extremely worried. Why not change the method slightly? I heard from the river workers that there were quite a few people with knowledge, but due to the difficult environment, it was difficult to take action. I was heartbroken when I witnessed this and could not bear to sit idly by. The fellow villagers from various counties knew that I had knowledge of the new method of repairing breaches at the Gongjia Dam on the Yellow River, which was effective, and urged me to ask the provincial authorities to use the easier method to rush to repair the breach in order to save lives. I met Chairman Ye, but before I could speak, Chairman Ye blurted out first, asking if there was any method to repair the breach and asking about the truth of the Gongjia Dam project. I told him everything, and he firmly asked me to invite the person to inspect the situation and hoped to implement it as soon as possible to alleviate the people's difficulties. He said with concern and tears that the water damage was his fault. Driven by my conscience and duty, I resolutely sought to help. I arrived in Shanghai on the 6th and immediately invited Zhuo Jingsan, an engineer who had worked at the Gongjia Dam, and he invited his colleagues, foreign engineer Gaulke and Chinese technician Wan Kaijia. The three of them are now running the Yitai Construction Company. They urged me to go together that night because disaster relief is more urgent than fighting a fire. We arrived in Zhenjiang at 5:00 AM on the 7th and were picked up by personnel sent by the provincial government to the Dahua Hotel to wait for Chairman Jiang to return from Beijing. After meeting and discussing everything, we immediately set off. The provincial government sent Li Yuting to accompany us, and the Department of Construction sent Lu Rixiang and Zhu Taixin to follow us in order to contact and consult along the way. We first arrived at the Xiaoxiantang in Shaobo, a small breach, which was under construction, but the entire town was severely damaged. Looking east, it was a vast ocean, reflecting the West Lake. Going north to Zhaoguan Dam, the dam foundation was still solid, but the east side was breached by dozens of feet. Several miles further north was the Lotus Pond at the Xiankou, which was more than a hundred feet wide, but the water flow was not as rapid as at Zhaoguan Dam. After arriving at Gaoyou, we went around the west embankment and climbed north, crossing to the breach at the Dangjunlou, where the water勢 was rushing and dangerous, more dangerous than the Sichuan River. The waves were surging, and the sound could be heard for several miles. Looking east, the water was over the rooftops, and some of the tiled houses were still sturdy, their tops resisting the waves. To the south of this breach was the breach at Miaoxiangkou, where the water was slower, with an uncollapsed embankment in the middle. These two locations were estimated to be 200 feet wide, and the west embankment was damaged for about 1,000 feet. After half a day of research by the engineers, it was estimated that if the transportation of soil and stone could be well organized and delivered on time and in the required amount, the project could be completed in two months. Thousands of disaster victims gathered on the embankment, hearing the news and crying, begging to be realized as soon as possible, in an extremely tragic state. On the way back to Zhenjiang, we looked for places to extract soil, with Wantou being the most suitable. If it was not enough, we would have to take it from Zhenjiang. We reported to Chairman Ye at noon on the 9th. At the same time, Director Wu Tongju was also present. He was told that the River Works Department and Mr. Wan Xiaoan, who had a wealth of experience in river management, believed that there was really no way to deal with the dangerous breach at Dangjunlou at this time. He also believed that the success of the new method at Gongjia Dam was reliable. At that time, it was decided to ask the engineers to return to Shanghai immediately, collect the equipment, and go to the site for actual measurement as soon as possible to prepare a plan for benefit. Chairman Ye repeatedly stated that the National Government is the people's government. At this time, it is necessary to save lives, and the cost will be borne by him. If there are really difficulties, he will be satisfied if it can be completed in three months. In short, the faster the better. The engineers also said that human beings should have compassion for each other and help each other. As long as their ability allows, they are willing to fulfill their obligations and complete this great project. We arrived in Shanghai that night. I and the engineers all suffered from diarrhea on the way. I could go despite my illness, but the others needed a doctor's examination. After repeated discussions, it was agreed to take a special express train at 10:00 AM tomorrow. If this trip can be implemented, I hope that the fellow villagers in the disaster-stricken counties will quickly organize an assistance group to help collect soil and stones and supervise transportation so that construction can be completed on schedule. If each county sends four people to be responsible for management, and each county can provide dozens of boats to help transport, paying wages, it is not difficult to do. It is hoped that they will work hard to supervise and help the government and the people cooperate to overcome this difficulty. It is also hoped that they will work together to study methods to permanently eliminate floods. We cannot wash them away once every 60 years. I hope all fellow villagers will pay attention. Today, I also met Mr. Cheng Jingsheng, who is also very willing to help. I also heard from the old river management expert, Mr. Wang Shuxiang, that there is no way to deal with the dangerous breach at Dangjunlou. Now that there is a way, as long as everyone supervises and helps, later someone suggested that if it can be completed on schedule as Mr. Shen said, the people of the lower counties should build a temple for each of them and worship them forever. Shen said that the Kuomintang's doctrine is to reduce the suffering of the people and increase the welfare of the people. We members should have this courage and do our best to achieve it. Who would build a clay puppet to be overthrown by others? The meeting dispersed with laughter.

Liu Ruiheng's Report on Epidemic Prevention in Wuhan 132

The Health and Epidemic Prevention Group of the National Government's Flood Relief Committee began its work after departing from the committee in Wuhan on the 18th of last month. Liu Ruiheng, the director of the group, reported on the work of the group as follows: Our group began its work after arriving in Wuhan on August 10th. We organized a team of health inspectors with police officers and school students, and sent them to work in various shelters. Regarding vaccinations to prevent typhoid fever and cholera, we can administer about 5,000 vaccinations per day. We also implemented clean drinking water and disposal of sewage in the larger shelters. As for medical relief, we used mobile clinics to meet the needs. Currently, the work in the disaster area is only in the Wuhan area, with particular emphasis on shelters with more than 1,000 people. In the future, the health and epidemic prevention equipment of our group will follow the work of the disaster area working group. Maintaining health and protection is as important as providing shelter, food, and drink for disaster victims. Therefore, the most important goals of our group are: (1) to do our best to prevent the spread of epidemics; (2) to remove all unhygienic filth to create a hygienic environment; and (3) to use medical relief equipment to reduce suffering and death. What is even more encouraging is that all parties have expressed their willingness to cooperate with our group in this plan to complete it. For example, (1) the South Manchuria Railway Company is willing to use a ship as an office for health work in the disaster area, and as a storage place for medical supplies. At the same time, a laboratory and pharmacy can be set up; (2) the Shanghai International Relief Committee will hire the Hanamalie ship as a hospital ship, and the Rastoel Institute will set up a laboratory on this ship; (3) governments, charities, and pharmaceutical companies from various countries have donated medical and health supplies. The detailed numbers will be announced separately in the coming days; (4) Most of the positions are filled by doctors, nurses, and sanitation engineers transferred from the Ministry of Health. The Medical College of Central University, Peking Union Medical College, the Chinese Red Cross, and the Japanese Red Cross Society have all had staff members who have gone to Wuhan for work under the guidance of our group. Church doctors across the country have also been notified to join the collaboration. Major hospitals and medical schools have also sent investigation forms requesting volunteers to be completed and returned. The minimum term for this volunteer work is two months. As for the doctors and nurses in Wuhan, they are cooperating with our group and, in addition to their support, their hospital addresses and all equipment can be used, which is especially convenient.

All Sectors Enthusiastically Contribute to Relief 135

▲ The Tea and Food Industry Raised More Than 3,200 Yuan:

Wang Renhe, Laoda Fang, Laoda Fang Branch, Xin Dian, Nanbei Tianlu, Lao Dachang, Shenshengchang, Daoxiangcun, Yezizhai, Huashengxing, Nanshi Daoxiangcun, Yezizhai, Shenshengchang, and the employees and workers of each store have donated generously. As of yesterday, more than 3,200 yuan has been raised. The association has allocated it to the provincial flood relief associations for distribution to the disaster areas.

▲ Negotiating with Shipping Bureau to Reduce Fees:

There are still more than 100,000 disaster victims in the Wuhan area. The relief association has consulted with various foreign shipping companies on the Yangtze River. For disaster victims traveling to Shanghai by ship, the ticket price will be uniformly reduced to half of the original price. The cost of food on board will also be reduced by one-half of the original price. It has been agreed upon.

▲ The Cotton Weaving Union Donated More Than 900 Yuan:

The Cotton Weaving Union in the Seventh District had previously resolved that each member should donate one day's wages and requested the factories to deduct the amount in advance and hand it over to the union for remittance to disaster relief. The factory has now calculated the amount, totaling more than 900 yuan, and will hand it over to the union负责人 for delivery within one or two days.

▲ Man and Woman Laborers Donate Hard-Earned Wages for Relief:

An old man from Jiangbei, Zhu, has lived in Pudong for a long time and is now 64 years old. He still carries water for a living, accumulating 50 yuan over the decades. Seeing the severe flood disaster in Jiangbei, he specially sent his life savings of 50 yuan to Li Rongji to be forwarded to the Yangzhou Eight Counties Fellow-Provincials Association and remitted to the disaster area. Li Qingyu, a merchant from Yangzhou who lives in Pudong, has a maid, Chou, whose wages are only four yuan. She also handed over her life savings of 20 yuan to the Yangzhou Eight Counties Fellow-Provincials Association to be remitted to the disaster area. The association considered the two donations to be rare and valuable and sent special letters of thanks and planned to prepare a reward area to encourage them.

▲ Customs Brokers Enthusiastically Provide Relief and Transportation:

The Customs Brokers Association sent a letter to the Disaster Relief Committee of Xu Shiying and Zhu Ziqiao, requesting them to designate a shelter that can accommodate 200 disaster victims, so that the association can directly provide food and drink to help the disaster victims.

▲ Female Doctor Provides Free Childbirth Services:

The Municipal Shelter for Disaster Victims received letters from Jianhua Hospital in Zhabei and female doctor Zhang Fujun, stating that if there are pregnant women among the disaster victims who are about to give birth, they can be sent for free childbirth services. However, there is a limit of 20-30 people per day, and medicine and other expenses will not be charged, and food rations will still be issued by the office.

▲ Six Civilian Ships Capsized in Shaobo:

In the Shaobo-Gaoyou flood disaster, dozens of small steamships from Suzhou, Wuxi, and Shanghai went to Jiangbei to transport disaster victims, and there were even more towed civilian boats. Yesterday, this city received a report from Yangzhou stating that six company and civilian ships carrying refugees were overturned by the waves in Shaobo at the same time. Boatmen and refugees all fell into the water. Fortunately, they were rescued by accompanying ships, but the ships were mostly damaged. There is no news that the small steamers have been released.

Jiangyuan Warship of the First Fleet Runs Aground in Xinghua 137

Accident Caused by Pursuit of Pirates

All Officers and Soldiers Rescued

▲ Departing to Suppress Bandits: The Jiangyuan warship of the First Naval Fleet was on patrol in the waters off Zhejiang and Fujian. On the afternoon of the 8th of this month, at 2:00 PM, the warship discovered pirate vessels in Xinghua Bay, Fujian. The Jiangyuan warship advanced towards the pirates, who fled into Xinghua Bay. The Jiangyuan pursued, intending to capture them in one fell swoop. However, the pirates were familiar with the sea, their boats were small, and the bay had many hidden reefs. As a result, the Jiangyuan ran aground.

▲ Runs Aground on a Hidden Reef: The Jiangyuan warship entered Xinghua Bay, where navigation was very difficult. At 2:30 PM, the warship ran aground on a hidden reef. The bottom of the ship was pierced by the reef, and seawater entered the cabin. After the accident, it was impossible to move the ship off the reef. The captain sent a radio message for help.

▲ Ten Warships Search: Commander Chen Jiliang of the First Fleet was anxious because he had not heard from the Jiangyuan warship after it pursued the pirates and it had not returned to the fleet. He immediately ordered ten warships under his command to search the sea in different directions. Later, he received a telegram informing him that the Jiangyuan had run aground in Xinghua Bay and sent warships to rescue it.

▲ Technicians Go to Fujian for Rescue: Because the warships could not tow the Jiangyuan, a telegram was sent to the Shanghai Naval Headquarters, contacting the Mitsui & Co. tugboat company in Shanghai. Yesterday, Mitsui sent technician Bentake, along with divers, aboard the Osaka Company's Changsha Maru to Fujian to inspect the situation and determine a salvage plan.

▲ Officers and Soldiers Rescued: Yesterday, Shanghai received confirmation that the officers, soldiers, and crew of the Jiangyuan warship had been rescued by the rescue warship. The ship's hull will be inspected by technicians at a later date to determine a towing plan. The Jiangyuan warship has a displacement of 700 tons and was built by Mitsubishi Shipyard in Japan 25 years ago.

Page 15

Local News Two

Eight-Year-Old Child Yao Jusheng Missing 140

Kidnapped by Bandits

Ransom Note Demands 20,000 Yuan

Two Male and Female Bandits Arrested

Child's Whereabouts Still Unknown

Yao Gu, a local woman residing at No. 199 Ma'an Lane, Chongqing Road, is 25 years old and a widow with an eight-year-old son named Jusheng, who is exceptionally lively. Around 3:00 PM on July 7th of this year, Yao Gu led her son to visit her mother, Gu Zhao, at No. 96 Taihuai Lane, Annam Road. Unexpectedly, Jusheng suddenly disappeared in front of the house. Searches were conducted everywhere, but it was as if he had sunk into the sea without a trace. By the 9th, Yao Gu's younger brother, Gu Peiheng, received an anonymous letter stating that Jusheng was safe and sound in a certain location and that they should not worry. After receiving the letter, the woman realized that her beloved son had fallen into the hands of bandits and was extremely anxious. However, because the bandits had not specified an address, there was no way to rescue him. Two days later, another letter arrived demanding a ransom of 20,000 yuan, stating that someone would be there to meet them if someone was sent to walk from Hartung Road to the Bund. The woman reported the incident to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, which ordered detectives to assist in the investigation. Yao Gu's mother, Gu Zhao, followed the instructions in the letter and walked to the Bund, with detectives following her in secret. However, the bandits did not appear. Several days later, another letter arrived, arranging a meeting at Zhengjia Wood Bridge. As expected, someone arrived to talk and was arrested by detectives and taken to the police station. Under interrogation, he confessed that his name was Tang Jinsheng, and he worked as a tea server at the Dong Sheng Hotel. He said that he had been entrusted with this matter by a guest named Li Jisan in room number one and that he did not know anything else. Chinese and Western detectives went to the hotel to investigate, but the so-called Li Jisan had already fled after hearing the news. It was determined that Tang was not actually involved in the case, so he was released. Several days ago, Yao Gu received another letter, arranging a meeting at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Henan Road at 9:00 AM the day before. She reported the incident to the police, who ordered Chinese detective Jin Yangwu to lead four detectives disguised as rickshaw pullers to the designated location to wait. Gu Zhao, Yao Gu's mother, carried a paper package resembling 20,000 yuan in cash and paced back and forth at the location. Around 10:00 AM, a person arrived in a rickshaw driven by Li Xiaokun from Li Xiaodi Kun. Seeing Gu Zhao carrying the paper package and walking back and forth on the opposite side, he instructed the rickshaw puller Li Xiaokun to go forward and retrieve the package. Li, unaware of the contents, took the paper package from Gu Zhao's hand and handed it over. Just as he was about to pull the rickshaw and run, the detectives, who had witnessed everything, rushed forward and arrested both the rickshaw puller and the passenger, taking them to the Jing'an Temple Police Station. The passenger identified himself as Zhu Songlin from Pudong, admitted to being involved in the case, and stated that the child Yao Jusheng was currently at the home of a Suzhou woman named Lu Wang (also known as Sister Er or Little Aunt) at No. 20 Ma Tianxing Lane, Nanshi. Chinese and Western detectives took Mr. Zhu to the Public Security Bureau to join the detectives and arrest Lu Wang. However, the child's whereabouts remain unknown. When questioned, she firmly denied the charges. Both were taken back to the police station and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special District Court, where Judge Wu Tingqi interrogated them. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the police station, presented the above information, stating that Zhu Songlin, also known as Li Jisan, could be proven by the tea server Tang Jinsheng and that Zhu had previously been a tenant of Gu Zhao, so he knew the situation in Yao Gu's home. However, last month, someone impersonated a bandit and attempted to extort 96 yuan from Yao Gu. The case was discovered, and the person was arrested and sent to the Summary Court, where he was sentenced to two months of imprisonment. Since the child Yao Jusheng has not yet been found, he requested a postponement. Tang Jinsheng, a tea server at the Dong Sheng Hotel, stated that Zhu Songlin arrived on July 15th, opened room number one, claimed to be Li Jisan, and said that a woman named Wang would be arriving, so the name Li Jisan, Li Wang was written in the circulation book. However, the woman never came. Three days later, Li suddenly ordered me to wait at the entrance of the Osmanthus Cake Shop at Zhengjia Wood Bridge, saying that if I saw an old woman wearing black pants and a white short shirt, I could ask her for a paper package containing clothes because the old woman was a relative of his and he was too ashamed to meet her. I was temporarily deceived and went to retrieve it on his behalf, but I was arrested by the detectives. Fortunately, after questioning, it was determined that I was not involved, so I was released, and other statements were made. Yao Gu and Gu Zhao also filed cases one after another, explaining everything. When questioned, Zhu Songlin confessed that he was not at the scene when Yao Jusheng was abducted, but he learned from Lu Wang and her sister Sister Xing (Sister San) and Li's lover Liu Ziyun that Jusheng was hidden at Lu Wang's home. Afterwards, I sent two letters to Yao Gu's home from Hankou and Yichang and admitted to sending people to retrieve the money twice. When questioned, Lu Wang, who runs a brothel, denied abducting Yao Jusheng and hiding him at her home, as well as the extortion. After reviewing the statements, Judge Wu ordered both defendants to be remanded in custody separately and wait for a postponement for further investigation and interrogation.

Bandit Gang Members Fight 141

Many Male and Female Robbers Arrested

The serious case of bandits and the Security Corps exchanging gunfire occurred on Xieshi Road, Nanshi, the night before last (the 8th). Two members of the Corps were wounded on the spot. Since then, many bandits have been captured one after another. The details are as follows:

▲ Six People Act Suspicious: Xieshi Road, Nanshi, is under the jurisdiction of the Second District General Office, where the Third Defense Unit of the Fifth Team of the First Regiment of the Shanghai Nanshi Security Corps is stationed. The night before last, members of the team finished their training at 8:00 PM and returned home. A squad leader, along with Zhao Zhenfu and Zhang Shanbao, were walking when they suddenly spotted six suspicious-looking men near a street corner at a certain temple bridge. The squad leader shouted a password, but the men suddenly drew pistols and fired at the Corps members.

▲ Two Corps Members Wounded: When the Corps members saw the men firing, they also took down rifles from their shoulders and returned fire. However, it was too late. Zhao and Zhang were each shot and fell to the ground. At the time, the police chief of the New West District of the Second District General Office of the Public Security Bureau happened to be on patrol. He suddenly heard the sound of gunfire and shouts of "robbery." He immediately surrounded the area and captured a robber near a small river.

▲ Bandits Arrested One After Another: Zhao and Zhang were rushed to the hospital for treatment. The captured robber was taken to the station and identified as Chen Zhengying. He said that his accomplices were hiding in a kiosk at No. 36 Yinyu Lane, Baxianqiao. Director Wang obtained the information and immediately ordered detectives to work with the police to arrest Wang Haiqing at the address. Wang had a gunshot wound on the left side of his neck, and there was blood on the bedding, indicating a rifle bullet wound. Shortly after, many people, including the female bandit Wang Zhang, arrived one after another and were arrested one by one. A pistol was found on the female bandit Wang Zhang's person and was taken to the station for verification.

When this case occurred, this newspaper received the news immediately. We originally intended to disclose it the following day, but at the request of District Member Wang of the Second District General Office, we temporarily refrained from publishing it to facilitate the investigation of accomplices. This newspaper, out of respect for District Member Wang's opinion, did not publish it until now. However, other newspapers have already published it, so we are supplementing the facts as above.

First Special District Court to Build a Foreign Tribunal 142

Building a Five-Story Cement Building

Bidding for Construction Begins Immediately

The number of civil and criminal cases handled by the Shanghai First Special District Court is increasing daily. After the formal abolition of consular jurisdiction in China by various countries on January 1st of next year, all civil and criminal lawsuits involving foreigners in the Public Concession will be under the jurisdiction of the court. The Ministry of Justice has issued an order to prepare and organize a special tribunal to hear cases involving foreigners. Therefore, the court's courtroom and office space must be increased. Previously, due to the narrow address of the court, it was once planned to purchase civilian land in the East and West Districts to build separately. However, this was abandoned due to a lack of suitable locations and limited funds. Recently, it was decided to demolish the old building connected to the new building in the court and rebuild a five-story steel-concrete building. With this transformation, the height will be increased, and it will be used as a courtroom and office, which will be more than sufficient. Yesterday, President Yang reviewed the new building drawings and specifications prepared by the engineer and found them satisfactory. He immediately announced a call for bids for the construction. The bidding period runs from today until the 14th of this month. Any reliable construction company that has contracted to construct two projects worth over 100,000 taels is eligible to bid. The current location of the old building downstairs is the Document Section, and upstairs is the Sixth Tribunal. Once demolition begins, they will have to relocate temporarily.

Pudong Electric Company Promotes Business 146

Loans for Lighting

Rentals of Motors

Since last month, Pudong Electric Company has implemented a loan program for lighting. Those who cannot pay the installation fee in one lump sum can negotiate a loan with the company to be repaid in twelve months. The company does not charge for connecting electricity for users, and the number of deposits required is also very low. Therefore, for small users, for example, if three lights are needed, only a deposit of six yuan is required to enjoy the convenience of electric lights. As a result, small households in general are welcoming the program, and there is an endless stream of applications. It has been heard that the company is adopting a rental program for motors to promote electricity business, so that those who cannot purchase motors at one time can rent them from the company. The rental fees are very low, only enough to offset interest and depreciation losses, and they do not seek any profit. The program has been submitted to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau for approval and record. Motors ranging from one horsepower to fifty horsepower are available in stock and can be rented at any time. If a user uses a lot of electricity and can guarantee a certain amount of electricity usage per horsepower per month, they can negotiate with the company to reduce or completely waive the rental fee. These motors are purchased in large quantities from the manufacturers, so their value is lower than purchasing them retail on the market. If a user wishes to purchase one, they can be sold at the original price. If they cannot pay in one lump sum, they can pay in installments. If the user is unclear about the installation and management methods of the motor, the company can design and send personnel to guide them.

Changed to Municipal Treasury Expenditure

Since the meat merchants in the Jiangwan District were approved to establish slaughterhouses in the district, they are exempt from merging the slaughter and inspection of pigs and sheep. In order to sympathize with the meat merchants, it has been approved by the Municipal Health Bureau to be approved by the Municipal Government. From July 20, the expenditure will be covered by the municipal treasury, and all districts that have paid the office inspection fees for July will be returned. The receipts can be taken to the Health Bureau for collection.

Two Suspects in Zhu Chengzhang's Kidnapping Case Found Not Guilty 148

Li Sigong and Li Zhengtang were arrested by Lu Liankui, chief detective of the public police station, for suspected involvement in the kidnapping of Lu Shaotang. He was escorted to the First District Court for interrogation and detention. Li and others hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to defend them. They were acquitted after being declared innocent, but the police learned that the two Lis were also related to the kidnapping and murder of Zhu Chengzhang, president of the Guohuo Bank. They were re-prosecuted, and Li and others still hired lawyer Zhan as their defense counsel. The trial has lasted more than half a year, and the debate was reopened once. It was not until last Friday that it was concluded. Yesterday morning was the day for sentencing. Lawyer Zhan Jifeng, the defendant's defender, was also in court waiting for instructions. At 9:00 AM, Judge Feng Shide opened the Second Criminal Court and announced the verdict. The main text stated that Li Sigong and Li Zhengtang were both not guilty, and Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, also stated in court that he would not appeal against the two defendants and requested their release. The court approved the request.

Detective Team Intercepts Robbers 149

Mardy & Co. Exhibits New Studebaker Automobiles 151

Mardy & Co. at No. 10 Avenue Edward VII will exhibit new Studebaker automobiles from tomorrow onwards for public viewing. This car is completely revolutionary in automotive engineering. Automotive engineers have always wanted to eliminate the vibration of four-cylinder cars, but have never been able to achieve any effect. The Studebaker factory has first invented the principle of natural buoyancy, so the problem of vibration of four-cylinder cars can be solved satisfactorily. In addition, the Studebaker's free clutch is completely different from the free clutch of other cars. This car has a button on the dashboard. When the button is pressed, the car is free to start up. When the button is pulled out, the Klax and gear speed can be used again. Therefore, it can be fully used for free clutch at all forward speeds. As for the Klax, it is only used when starting and stopping the car. Its convenience is like this. It is expected that the public will hear the news and those who go to visit tomorrow will be very crowded.

Fujian Road Automatic Telephone Exchange Completed 154

To Be Activated on Sunday

The Public Concession Telephone Company has been converting to automatic exchanges, with a plan to complete the conversion within two years from last August. Now, at 321 Fujian Road, a new exchange building and equipment have been added and are ready. Starting Sunday, it will be put into use, becoming the third automatic exchange. The automatic telephone conversion project is thus taking a further step. The new Fujian Road exchange will serve 3,730 users, including 2,330 telephone lines originally connected to the Central District automatic exchange, 1,400 lines connected to the Central District manual exchange, and 30 lines connected to the Western District manual exchange. On Saturday night, all staff from the Central District and Fujian Road exchanges worked to implement the changes. At 1:00 AM on Sunday morning, the exchange began operations and connecting calls. A reporter was invited yesterday to visit and was guided by Mr. Fan, a training instructor, to inspect the various departments. The equipment is comprehensive and unparalleled. The Fujian Road exchange can accommodate 20,000 lines. The total cable length is 16,287 miles. The exchange equipment and telephone lines were manufactured by Antwerpen in Belgium.

Shanghai Exports to the US in August 155

Far Below the Previous Two Months

According to the Continental Times, Shanghai's exports to the United States in August were far less than in the previous two months. Goods subject to ad valorem duties by US Customs were valued at only US$1,086,632, with silk and silk products accounting for the largest share. Raw silk was valued at US$505,611, accounting for half of the total. Wild silk was US$19,564, waste silk was US$19,088, and pongee was US$16,391. There were also silk fabrics, lace, and other items with higher values. There were no exports of eggs, egg powder, or canned fish. Other animal products also sharply decreased. Silk and tea exports amounted to US$215,944, and black tea was US$6,064. The total value of exports to the US in the first eight months of this year was US$14,201,077. Shanghai's exports to the Philippines in August were valued at US$185,275, with fresh eggs and raw oil being the largest, valued at US$64,146 and US$18,697 respectively. Wheat flour was also valued at US$1,000. Shanghai's exports to Honolulu that month were only US$5,216.

Jiangxi Compatriot Association Asks for Careful Selection of Jiangxi Chairman 156

The Jiangxi Association in Shanghai sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang, Nanjing National Government: "To Chairman Chiang: Reports indicate that Chairman Lu of our province has repeatedly requested to resign, and your government is considering granting his request for rest. Our province has suffered from the Red disaster for several years, and it is difficult to eliminate and easy to revive. This has led to the gathering of large armies, and you have personally led the expedition in the summer heat. Although the root cause of the disaster lies in the cunning schemes of the bandits, the officials in charge have initially abandoned their responsibilities, allowing the bandits to spread rampant. Then, they have been ineffective in suppressing them, fostering a great calamity. Fortunately, relying on your power, the bandit forces have been greatly reduced. However, the remnants are scattered and may reignite. Without someone who understands the provincial situation and is willing to take responsibility, it will be difficult to achieve a fundamental cleanup. We implore your government to select a successor from among the capable and experienced individuals in our province who have been involved in bandit suppression and appoint them to the position. They will be deeply aware of the suffering and plan thoroughly, pursuing the roots of the problem without delay. This will complete your personal expedition and permanently eliminate the great disaster for our hometown. Otherwise, if a military officer from another province is lightly appointed to take over the responsibility, they will not be concerned about the suffering, and they will be timid and foster chaos, repeating the previous mistakes. The selection of personnel is of utmost importance. Our association, learning from past mistakes, offers its sincere advice. We beseech you to adopt it. The people of Jiangxi will be fortunate, and the whole country will be fortunate. Jiangxi Association in Shanghai."

Case of Chinese Electrical Company Employees Requesting Improved Treatment 157

Company Has Yet to Respond

Employees Will Take Action

All employees of the Chinese Electrical Company, due to difficult living conditions and unequal treatment, have specifically proposed eight articles for improving treatment and appointed Deng Shuping and eleven others as representatives to write to the company manager to schedule a joint signing. However, there has been no response for a long time. After deliberation by all employees, they jointly submitted a petition to the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau for mediation. Subsequently, the representatives received a No. 73 instruction from the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters, stating that the labor-capital agreement draft submitted by the representatives has been reviewed and corrected by the headquarters. In addition to sending a letter to the Social Affairs Bureau, they were instructed to follow the amended plan and sincerely negotiate with the management. The representatives immediately followed the amended labor-capital agreement draft and requested the company to schedule a meeting for negotiation again. However, Lu Bohong, the manager of the company, still has not made a firm statement on this matter. All employees believe that the company's business has experienced amazing expansion in recent years, but the manager has not made any effort to improve the difficult living conditions of the employees. Now, their reasonable demands have not been accepted with sincerity. They are extremely indignant. It is reported that the representatives, seeing the intense feelings of the employees, feel that they cannot maintain the situation. They have published a notice in the newspapers, stating that they will be responsible for another five days, from September 11th to 15th. During this period, they hope that the company manager will meet with the representatives to seriously negotiate and agree on the measures proposed by all employees to improve treatment, in order to appease public anger. If the company continues to ignore the issue or if other complications arise, the representatives will not be responsible. It is unknown what kind of response the company authorities will have upon seeing this.

Reader's Correspondence

Ms. Lan's Message

I am a lonely woman. I lost my father when I was nine years old. My father, on whom our family depended for a living, abandoned us halfway, and we suddenly lost our security and could no longer make a living. I was fortunate enough to be adopted by my aunt as a goddaughter. Since my aunt took me in, she has used her hard-earned salary to cultivate me to this day. I have gone from primary school to the second year of higher normal school. She survived a disaster and hopes that I will be able to support her for the rest of her life after I graduate. I am very timid at school and, apart from my studies, I am oblivious to everything else, because I am eagerly waiting to receive my diploma so that I can quickly earn money to support my elderly mother, comfort my hardworking aunt, and raise my two young beloved sisters. I feel the great responsibility and work even harder day and night. However, unfortunate people are always plagued by unfortunate events, putting me in a situation where I can neither live nor die. I have a cousin who is four years older than me, now twenty-one years old. He is very knowledgeable and has a good disposition, but unfortunately, he dropped out of school for the sake of his family. We played together since we were little, and when we were fifteen, we embarked on the path of true love. After two years of sacred love, he proposed marriage. He informed his parents several times, but his stubborn parents, disliking me for being a poor family's daughter, flatly refused. He argued vehemently but failed and was bedridden for a month, and repeatedly wanted to commit suicide to repay me. At the time, although I also hated the despotism of his family, I could not bear to cause a misfortune or even break up his happy family because of me alone, so I advised him to obey his parents and not to be a sinner against Confucianism. One woman's gain or loss is not worth being so passive. Although I comforted him with earnest words, he remained as passive as before. He is now being oppressed by a bad environment and has finally become engaged to his mother's niece. When he became engaged, he was still sick. After he recovered, the situation was a fait accompli and could not be reversed. But now, even though he is a married man, his love for me has not diminished at all. Sir, I am very confused now. Can I still love him? Can I still accept his control? I understand very well that his love is real, and if I stop loving him, he will be even more passive than he is now. But if this goes on, it will be like a small boat going out to sea with no turning back. Sir, please give me a clear path, I will be infinitely grateful. Because he also reads the newspaper every day, so just leaving a word Lan is enough.

(Reply) Since he (is a married man), you should of course not give your love to him again. Even if he still loves you, you must avoid suspicion. If his family develops resentment because of you, wouldn't you feel even more uneasy? Didn't you once advise him (not to cause a misfortune to the whole family because of me alone)? So from now on, you are loving him by not loving him.

Didn't you advise him (a woman's gain or loss is not worth being so passive)? Good, you are truly a woman of great integrity. You should also tell him, how great is the meaning of life, how great is the responsibility, how great is the future. Is it possible that a dignified man should spend his youth and good time in the sea of love between men and women, even if it is counted? Have you forgotten about school? Have you forgotten about service? Have you forgotten about your divine duty to the country and to society? You should also tell him, although I am a woman, from now on, I will go to school, I will serve, I do not want to completely bind the four limbs and five senses, which heaven and earth gave me and my parents nurtured, in a hazy and upside-down love network. I want to be a vigorous and promising citizen of the country and a member of society. You should say this to him very clearly and directly.

Message from Mr. Bao Jianxin

I am a high school graduate. Since graduation, due to circumstances, I have not been able to continue my studies. My temperament is close to the field of electrical engineering, so after dropping out of school, I have been groping around on my own. At the same time, I enrolled in a mechanical engineering course at an American correspondence school. At that time, tuition was only five yuan per month. Later, due to money problems, I did not graduate, but except for a part of the factory practice textbook, I did not study, I finished reading the theoretical part. At the same time, I also read books on electricity and researched radio receivers (the Kailuo Company was just established at that time), and made applied instruments by hand. I have been doing this blindly for five years, and I have a lot of interest and experience. My current ability to make a living depends on this self-study. However, now I feel that (1) what I know is too superficial. If I spend my whole life in such a small power radio station, that's fine. But I hope to have development in the future and be able to go to an international radio station, then my knowledge is naturally not enough. I want to study further on my own, but the problem is that (2) my mathematics background is too shallow. I only learned trigonometry (I have not learned solid geometry and trigonometry). If I read a slightly more advanced book, I must understand calculus. Now I want to review algebra and trigonometry that I have already learned from the beginning, and then buy high school mathematics books in the bookstore, such as higher algebra, analytic geometry, and calculus. Which books are easy to self-study? (3) I want to find a factory practice position. On the one hand, I can increase my experience, and on the other hand, I can get closer to the engineering industry. I don't know if there is such an opportunity in Shanghai. (4) My goal of self-study is to obtain the academic ability to pass the electrical engineer qualification examination, so that I can have the qualification to be an engineer. If I can't become an engineer, I will achieve the academic qualification of an electrical engineering worker at a lower level no matter what. Can the gentleman give me a systematic reading list?

This issue is very important for the future of science and the training of scientific talents and should be the responsibility of the country. It is expected that the Department of Physics and Chemistry of the Academia Sinica will be able to undertake this task. Private institutions are limited by their expensive and limited power and cannot accommodate it, and the progress is slow. (3) Since you want to be an engineer, the purpose is not to take the exam. Postal Workers' Rice Subsidy Issue 158

Not a New Request

Based on Old Agreement

Due to the sudden increase in rice prices last year, the postal workers' union requested Wei Yihu, the former postmaster general, to forward the request to the Ministry of Communications for the issuance of rice subsidies. The method was to provide a subsidy of three yuan for those with a monthly salary of 50 yuan or less when the rice price was above 16 yuan, and two yuan for those with a monthly salary of more than 50 yuan but less than 80 yuan. The monthly salary was calculated excluding subsidies. It was decided to implement it from May 19th. At that time, former General Manager Wei and Dou Juecang, the current director of the Ministry of Communications, were responsible for the agreement. In April of this year, when the rice price fell below 16 yuan, the postal workers' union complied with the agreement and also agreed to stop the subsidy. However, in recent months, the rice price has gradually soared above 16 yuan again. According to the agreement, the General Administration should issue it as usual. Therefore, the postal workers' rice subsidy is not a new request. The report that the Ministry of Communications has rested is not true.

Preparations for the National Anti-Drug Representatives Conference 162

Set Up Preparation Offices in Different Regions

Send Personnel to Various Provinces to Promote

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association is actively proceeding with the convening of the National Anti-Drug Representatives Conference in accordance with the resolutions of the Standing Committee, and has decided that the conference will be held from November 1st to 5th of this year. The Zhejiang Provincial Party Headquarters in Hangzhou and the Hangzhou YMCA have been designated as the two venues. During the conference, it is planned to erect a monument to Premier Sun's anti-drug teachings in the name of all the representatives of the conference in the Sixth Park of West Lake in Hangzhou, as a permanent standard for drug prohibition. Regarding the travel of representatives, the Ministry of Railways has been requested to grant a half-price privilege, which will be issued by the conference preparatory office in the future for passage. All preparatory matters for the conference have been planned and actively handled. A conference preparatory office has been established at the Shanghai Chinese National Anti-Drug Association and the Hangzhou Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Drug Association. In addition, Northeast Preparation Office has been established at the Shenyang Liaoning Anti-Drug Association, North China Preparation Office has been established at the Tianjin Hebei Anti-Drug Association, South China Preparation Office has been established at the Fuzhou Fujian Anti-Drug Association, Southwest Preparation Office has been established at the Kunming Yunnan Anti-Drug Association, West China Preparation Office has been established at the Chengdu Sichuan Anti-Drug Association, East China Preparation Office has been established at the Hangzhou Zhejiang Anti-Drug Association, and Nanyang Preparation Office has been established at the Nanyang Singapore Anti-Drug Association. The directors of each office have also been separately appointed and will begin work immediately. On the one hand, the conference preparatory office will send special personnel to the Northeast, North China, South China, East China, and Nanyang regions to promote the mission of the conference, in order to arouse the sympathy of people across the country. In recent days, anti-drug groups from all over the world have been sending letters and telegrams to inquire about the details of the conference, and there must be many inquiries every day. It is reported that the conference preparatory office has now started to solicit proposals from various organizations and anti-drug groups, which will be submitted to the proposal review committee for review and then submitted to the conference. In addition, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association previously handled the memorial of Lin Gong Zexu forever based on the resolutions of the June 3 Memorial Conference. It has again requested the Hangzhou Municipal Government to allocate three rooms in the Pinghu Qiuyue Building in West Lake to serve as the Lin Zexu Memorial Hall to display anti-drug education exhibits. This undertaking has been negotiated several times by Chen Lingyun, the general manager of the Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Drug Association, and the Hangzhou authorities, and Huang Jiahui, the general manager of the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, has also gone to discuss it. In the future, a detailed plan will be submitted to the National Congress for approval, in order to establish a permanent memorial. Pinghu Qiuyue is one of the ten famous scenic spots in West Lake. In the future, it will be used to commemorate the anti-drug pioneers, which can be said to be suitable for both people and places.
